struct PositionData
{
   string Table;
   int PositionID;
   double TP;
   double SL;
   double TrailTP;
   double TrailThresh;
   double Lots;
   datetime OrderTime;
   string Side;
   int OriginalID;
   string symbol;
   int OrderNum;
   int StratNum;
   double Price;
   datetime ExpiryDate;
   double Nums[20]; // Array for Num1 to Num20
};

struct TempPositionData
{
   string Table;
   int PositionID;
   double TP;
   double SL;
   double TrailTP;
   double TrailThresh;
   double Lots;
   datetime OrderTime;
   string Side;
   int OriginalID;
   string symbol;
   int OrderNum;
   int StratNum;
   double Price;
   datetime ExpiryDate;
   double Nums[20]; // Array for Num1 to Num20
};

enum ENUM_POS_SIZE_METHOD
{
   MIN_LOT_SIZE,                                //Minimum Lot Size ('Broker min lots' for symbol used)
   FIXED_LOT_SIZE,                              //Fixed Lot Size (Specify the lot size to use)
   RELATIVE_LOT_SIZE                            //Relative Lot Size (Relative to Equity)
};
enum ENUM_CUSTOM_PERF_CRITERIUM_METHOD
{
   NO_CUSTOM_METRIC,                            //No Custom Metric
   STANDARD_PROFIT_FACTOR,                      //Standard Profit Factor
   MODIFIED_PROFIT_FACTOR,                      //Modified Profit Factor
   CAGR_OVER_MEAN_DD,                           //CAGR/MeanDD
   COEFF_CORRELATION_R,                          //Coefficient of Correlation (r)
   MODIFIED_PROFIT_FACTORANDCOEFF_CORRELATION_R
};
enum ENUM_DIAGNOSTIC_LOGGING_LEVEL
{
   DIAG_LOGGING_NONE,                           //NONE
   DIAG_LOGGING_LOW,                            //LOW - Major Diagnostics Only
   DIAG_LOGGING_MEDIUM,                         //MEDIUM - Medium level logging
   DIAG_LOGGING_HIGH                            //HIGH - All Diagnostics (Warning - Use with caution)
};

ENUM_POS_SIZE_METHOD                PositionSizingMethod   = RELATIVE_LOT_SIZE;        //Position Sizing Method

ENUM_DIAGNOSTIC_LOGGING_LEVEL       DiagnosticLoggingLevel = DIAG_LOGGING_NONE;         //Diagnostic Logging Level

//Globals
int      PreviousHourlyTasksRun  = -1;          //Set to -1 so that hourly tasks run immediately
double   EquityHistoryArray[];                  //Used to store equity at intermittent time intervals when using the Strategy Tester in order to calculate CAGR/MeanDD perf metric
double   StartingEquity;                        //Stores the Starting Equity (i.e. the deposit amount at the beginning of the backtest)
datetime BackTestFirstDate;                     //Used in the CAGR/MeanDD Calc
datetime BackTestFinalDate;                     //Used in the CAGR/MeanDD Calc


enum LOT_MODE_ENUM{
   LOT_MODE_FIXED,
   LOT_MODE_MONEY,
   LOT_MODE_PERCENTAGE_ACCOUNT
};

bool ValidateInputsGeneral()
{
   if(baseOrderSizeMultiplyer < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: baseOrderSizeMultiplyer must be >= 0. Got: ", baseOrderSizeMultiplyer);
      return false;
   }
      if(max_orders < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: max_orders must be >= 1. Got: ", max_orders);
      return false;
   }
      if(drawdownThreshold_percentage < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: drawdownThreshold_percentage must be >= 0. Got: ", drawdownThreshold_percentage);
      return false;
   }
         if(drawdownThreshold_percentage > 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: drawdownThreshold_percentage must not be > 1. Got: ", drawdownThreshold_percentage);
      return false;
   }
      if(drawdownThreshold_percentage_OPEN < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: drawdownThreshold_percentage_OPEN must be >= 0. Got: ", drawdownThreshold_percentage_OPEN);
      return false;
   }
      if(drawdownThreshold_percentage_OPEN > 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: drawdownThreshold_percentage_OPEN must not be > 1. Got: ", drawdownThreshold_percentage_OPEN);
      return false;
   }
   
      
   if(StringLen(folderName) == 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: Terminal storage folder name needs to be something: ", folderName);
      return false;
   }
   if(StringLen(folderName_c) == 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: Common storage folder name needs to be something: ", folderName_c);
      return false;
   }

   if(MAGIC_NUMBER < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: MAGIC_NUMBER must be >= 1. Got: ", MAGIC_NUMBER);
      return false;
   }

   if(update_counter_input < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: update_counter_input must be >= 1. Got: ", update_counter_input);
      return false;
   }

   if(RecordingInterval < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: RecordingInterval must be >= 1. Got: ", RecordingInterval);
      return false;
   }
   if(RecordingInterval > 100000)
   {
      Print("Init Error: RecordingInterval must be <= 100000. Got: ", RecordingInterval);
      return false;
   }
   
   if(countdownInterval < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: countdownInterval must be >= 1. Got: ", countdownInterval);
      return false;
   }
      if(countdownInterval > 1000)
   {
      Print("Init Error: countdownInterval must be <= 1000. Got: ", countdownInterval);
      return false;
   }
      if(CheckTradesWithinLast < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: CheckTradesWithinLast must be >= 1. Got: ", CheckTradesWithinLast);
      return false;
   }
      if(CheckTradesWithinLast > 10000)
   {
      Print("Init Error: CheckTradesWithinLast must be <= 10000. Got: ", CheckTradesWithinLast);
      return false;
   }
   
   if(StringLen(CheckTradesWithinLastSymbol) == 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: open a trade every number of days symbol used needs to be something ", CheckTradesWithinLastSymbol);
      return false;
   }   

   return true;
}

bool ValidateInputs8()
{

   if(StringLen(comment8_input) == 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: comment8_input comment needs to be something: ", comment8_input);
      return false;
   }

   if(spreadPercent_thresh8 < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: spreadPercent_thresh8 must be > 0. Got: ", spreadPercent_thresh8);
      return false;
   }

   if(strat8OrderSizeMultiplyer < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: strat8OrderSizeMultiplyer must be > 0. Got: ", strat8OrderSizeMultiplyer);
      return false;
   }

   if(max_trades8 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: max_trades8 must be >= 1. Got: ", max_trades8);
      return false;
   }
   if(update_counter_input8 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: update_counter_input8 must be >= 1. Got: ", update_counter_input8);
      return false;
   }
      if(average_PERIOD8 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: average_PERIOD8 must be >= 1. Got: ", average_PERIOD8);
      return false;
   }
      if(stop_loss_pct8 < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: stop_loss_pct8 must be >= 0. Got: ", stop_loss_pct8);
      return false;
   }
   if(stop_loss_pct8 > 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: stop_loss_pct8 must be < 1. Got: ", stop_loss_pct8);
      return false;
   }
   
      if(envelope_1_pct < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: envelope_1_pct must be >= 0. Got: ", envelope_1_pct);
      return false;
   }
      if(envelope_2_pct < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: envelope_2_pct must be >= 0. Got: ", envelope_2_pct);
      return false;
   }
         if(envelope_3_pct < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: envelope_3_pct must be >= 0. Got: ", envelope_3_pct);
      return false;
   }
      if(envelope_1_pct > 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: envelope_1_pct must be < 1. Got: ", envelope_1_pct);
      return false;
   }
      if(envelope_2_pct > 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: envelope_2_pct must be < 1. Got: ", envelope_2_pct);
      return false;
   }
         if(envelope_3_pct > 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: envelope_3_pct must be < 1. Got: ", envelope_3_pct);
      return false;
   }   
   
   return true;
}

bool ValidateInputs13()
{
   // Check string input
   if(StringLen(comment13_input) == 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: comment13_input must not be empty.");
      return false;
   }

   // Double values expected to be >= 0
   if(spreadPercent_thresh13 < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: spreadPercent_thresh13 must be >= 0. Got: ", spreadPercent_thresh13);
      return false;
   }

   if(strat13OrderSizeMultiplyer < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: strat13OrderSizeMultiplyer must be >= 0. Got: ", strat13OrderSizeMultiplyer);
      return false;
   }

   if(InpLots_L13 < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: InpLots_L13 must be >= 0. Got: ", InpLots_L13);
      return false;
   }

   // Integer/ulong values expected to be >= 1
   if(max_trades13 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: max_trades13 must be >= 1. Got: ", max_trades13);
      return false;
   }

   if(update_counter_input13 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: update_counter_input13 must be >= 1. Got: ", update_counter_input13);
      return false;
   }

   if(length13 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: length13 must be >= 1. Got: ", length13);
      return false;
   }

   if(ci_thresh13 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: ci_thresh13 must be >= 1. Got: ", ci_thresh13);
      return false;
   }

   if(ADXlength13 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: ADXlength13 must be >= 1. Got: ", ADXlength13);
      return false;
   }

   if(adx_value_thresh13 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: adx_value_thresh13 must be >= 1. Got: ", adx_value_thresh13);
      return false;
   }

   if(ATRinput13 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: ATRinput13 must be >= 1. Got: ", ATRinput13);
      return false;
   }

   if(sl_atr_multi13 < 0 || tp_atr_multi13 < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: sl_atr_multi13 and tp_atr_multi13 must be >= 0. Got: SL=", sl_atr_multi13, ", TP=", tp_atr_multi13);
      return false;
   }

   if(bands_period13 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: bands_period13 must be >= 1. Got: ", bands_period13);
      return false;
   }

   if(BB_deveation13 <= 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: BB_deveation13 must be > 0. Got: ", BB_deveation13);
      return false;
   }

   if(bbw_thresh13 < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: bbw_thresh13 must be >= 0. Got: ", bbw_thresh13);
      return false;
   }

   if(tenkan_sen13 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: tenkan_sen13 must be >= 1. Got: ", tenkan_sen13);
      return false;
   }

   if(kijun_sen13 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: kijun_sen13 must be >= 1. Got: ", kijun_sen13);
      return false;
   }

   if(senkou_span_b13 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: senkou_span_b13 must be >= 1. Got: ", senkou_span_b13);
      return false;
   }

   return true;
}

{
   // String input check
   if(StringLen(comment4_input) == 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: comment4_input must not be empty.");
      return false;
   }

   // Double values expected to be >= 0
   if(spreadPercent_thresh4 < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: spreadPercent_thresh4 must be >= 0. Got: ", spreadPercent_thresh4);
      return false;
   }

   if(strat4OrderSizeMultiplyer < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: strat4OrderSizeMultiplyer must be >= 0. Got: ", strat4OrderSizeMultiplyer);

   }

   if(InpLots_L4 < 0)

      Print("Init Error: InpLots_L4 must be >= 0. Got: ", InpLots_L4);
      return false;
   }

   // Integer / ulong checks

   {
      Print("Init Error: max_trades4 must be >= 1. Got: ", max_trades4);
      return false;
   }

   if(update_counter_input4 < 1)

      Print("Init Error: update_counter_input4 must be >= 1. Got: ", update_counter_input4);
      return false;
   }

   if(EMA_PERIOD4 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: EMA_PERIOD4 must be >= 1. Got: ", EMA_PERIOD4);
      return false;
   }

   if(ATRinput4 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: ATRinput4 must be >= 1. Got: ", ATRinput4);
      return false;
   }

   if(sl_atr_multi4 < 0)
   {
      Print("Init Error: sl_atr_multi4 must be >= 0. Got: ", sl_atr_multi4);
      return false;
   }

   // Stochastic periods
   if(Stochastic_slowing4 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: Stochastic_slowing4 must be >= 1. Got: ", Stochastic_slowing4);
      return false;
   }

   if(Stochastic_D_period4 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: Stochastic_D_period4 must be >= 1. Got: ", Stochastic_D_period4);
      return false;
   }

   if(Stochastic_k_period4 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: Stochastic_k_period4 must be >= 1. Got: ", Stochastic_k_period4);
      return false;
   }

   // MACD periods
   if(fast_macd_period4 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: fast_macd_period4 must be >= 1. Got: ", fast_macd_period4);
      return false;
   }

   if(slow_macd_period4 < 1)

      Print("Init Error: slow_macd_period4 must be >= 1. Got: ", slow_macd_period4);
      return false;
   }

   if(macd_signal_period4 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: macd_signal_period4 must be >= 1. Got: ", macd_signal_period4);
      return false;
   }

   return true;
}

   if(update_counter_input5 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: update_counter_input5 must be >= 1. Got: ", update_counter_input5);
      return false;
   }

   if(ATRinput5 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: ATRinput5 must be >= 1. Got: ", ATRinput5);
      return false;
   }

   if(barsToCheck < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: barsToCheck must be >= 1. Got: ", barsToCheck);
      return false;
   }

   if(RSIPeriod5 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: RSIPeriod5 must be >= 1. Got: ", RSIPeriod5);
      return false;
   }

   // Stochastic periods
   if(Stochastic_slowing5 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: Stochastic_slowing5 must be >= 1. Got: ", Stochastic_slowing5);
      return false;
   }

   if(Stochastic_D_period5 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: Stochastic_D_period5 must be >= 1. Got: ", Stochastic_D_period5);
      return false;
   }

   if(Stochastic_k_period5 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: Stochastic_k_period5 must be >= 1. Got: ", Stochastic_k_period5);
      return false;
   }

   // MACD periods
   if(fast_macd_period5 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: fast_macd_period5 must be >= 1. Got: ", fast_macd_period5);
      return false;
   }

   if(slow_macd_period5 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: slow_macd_period5 must be >= 1. Got: ", slow_macd_period5);
      return false;
   }

   if(macd_signal_period5 < 1)
   {
      Print("Init Error: macd_signal_period5 must be >= 1. Got: ", macd_signal_period5);
      return false;
   }

   return true;
}

// Check and add symbol to Market Watch if needed
bool EnsureSymbolAvailable(string symbol)
{
   if(!SymbolInfoInteger(symbol, SYMBOL_EXIST))
   {
      Print("Symbol does not exist in terminal: ", symbol);
      return false;
   }

   if(SymbolInfoInteger(symbol, SYMBOL_SELECT))
      return true;

   if(!SymbolSelect(symbol, true))
   {
      Print("Failed to select symbol: ", symbol);
      return false;
   }

   return true;
}

int OnInit()
{

   Print("---------------------- starting ----------------------");
   
   
   Print("WannaBeQuant strategy selection version ", version);
   
   if(!ValidateInputsGeneral()){return(INIT_FAILED);}
   if(!ValidateInputs8()){return(INIT_FAILED);}
   //if(!ValidateInputs6()){return(INIT_FAILED);}
   if(!ValidateInputs13()){return(INIT_FAILED);}
   if(!ValidateInputs11()){return(INIT_FAILED);}
   if(!ValidateInputs3()){return(INIT_FAILED);}
   if(!ValidateInputs4()){return(INIT_FAILED);}
   if(!ValidateInputs5()){return(INIT_FAILED);}
   //if(!ValidateInputs12()){return(INIT_FAILED);}
   
   record_equity = true ;
   backtest_active = false ;
   if(MQLInfoInteger(MQL_TESTER)){
      record_equity = false ;
      backtest_active = true ;
   }
   

   
   CreatePositionTables(dbFile);
   
   //DeleteOldDatabase("SentimentData.db");
   
   trade.SetExpertMagicNumber(MAGIC_NUMBER);
   

   ulong positionIDList[];  // Array to store PositionID values

   // Retrieve table names
   //GetTableNames(dbFile, tableList);

   // Retrieve all PositionID values from all tables
   GetAllPositionIDs(dbFile, positionIDList);
   
      // Print the retrieved PositionIDs
   Print("Retrieved PositionIDs: ", ArraySize(positionIDList));
   for (int i = 0; i < ArraySize(positionIDList); i++)
   {
      //Print("PositionID[", i, "]: ", positionIDList[i]);
      
      if (PositionSelectByTicket(positionIDList[i])) 
      {
         Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", positionIDList[i]);
      }
      else
      {
         int arraydelete[1];
         arraydelete[0] = positionIDList[i];
         Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting... ", positionIDList[i]);
         DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
      }
      
   }
   
   
   ulong positionList[];  // Array to store Position IDs
   ulong orderList[];  // Array to store Order IDs

   // Retrieve active positions and orders
   GetActivePositionsAndOrders(MAGIC_NUMBER, positionList, orderList);
   
   ulong missingIDs[];  // Array to store missing trade IDs

   // Find missing trade IDs
   FindMissingTradeIDs(positionIDList, positionList, orderList, missingIDs);

   // Print missing IDs
   if(ArraySize(missingIDs)>0){
      Print("ERROR Missing Trade IDs EA will not run withought closing trades or adding them to sqlite table file");
      for (int i = 0; i < ArraySize(missingIDs); i++)
      {
         Print("ERROR Missing ID: ", missingIDs[i], " Fix by 1. adding position to correct sqlite table or 2. close order Manually");
      }
      
      return(INIT_FAILED); 
   }


//   string TradeSymbolsToUse = "";
//   
//   if(TradeSymbols == "ALL")
//      TradeSymbolsToUse = AllSymbolsString;
//   else
//      TradeSymbolsToUse = TradeSymbols;
//   
//   //CONVERT TradeSymbolsToUse TO THE STRING ARRAY SymbolArray
//   NumberOfTradeableSymbols = StringSplit(AllSymbolsString, '|', SymbolArray);
   


   if(MQLInfoInteger(MQL_TESTER))
   {
      if(PositionSizingMethod == RELATIVE_LOT_SIZE && CustomPerfCriterium == STANDARD_PROFIT_FACTOR)
      {
         Print("You have attempted to test the EA in the Strategy Tester using a RELATIVE_LOT_SIZE which is not compatible with the CustomPerfCriterium of STANDARD_PROFIT_FACTOR (Trades when equity is high have a disproportionate effect on the Profit Factor calculation than trades taken when equity is low)");
         return(INIT_PARAMETERS_INCORRECT);
      }
      else if((PositionSizingMethod == MIN_LOT_SIZE || PositionSizingMethod == FIXED_LOT_SIZE) && CustomPerfCriterium == CAGR_OVER_MEAN_DD)
      {
         Print("You have attempted to test the EA in the Strategy Tester using " + EnumToString((ENUM_POS_SIZE_METHOD)PositionSizingMethod) + " which is not compatible with the CustomPerfCriterium of CAGR_OVER_MEAN_DD (The CAGR/MeanDD calculation requires position sizing relative to equity, in order to produce proportional drawdowns throughout the entire backtest)");
         return(INIT_PARAMETERS_INCORRECT);                                        
      }
   }
   
   //SET UP EQUITY HISTORY ARRAY AND FIRST DATE - USED TO CALCULATE CAGR/MeanDD
   if(MQLInfoInteger(MQL_TESTER))
   {
      BackTestFirstDate = TimeCurrent();
      ArrayResize(EquityHistoryArray, 1);    
      EquityHistoryArray[0] = AccountInfoDouble(ACCOUNT_EQUITY); 
   } 
   
//   ArrayResize(open_symbols, NumberOfTradeableSymbols);
//    ArrayResize(arrays, NumberOfTradeableSymbols);
//    
//   ArrayResize(array_min_load, NumberOfTradeableSymbols);
//   
//   ArrayResize(sentiment_N, NumberOfTradeableSymbols);
//   ArrayResize(sentiment_NEU, NumberOfTradeableSymbols);
//   ArrayResize(sentiment_P, NumberOfTradeableSymbols);
//   ArrayResize(total_percentage, NumberOfTradeableSymbols);
//   
//   ArrayResize(handle_atr1, NumberOfTradeableSymbols);
//   ArrayResize(handle_adx1, NumberOfTradeableSymbols);
//   ArrayResize(handle_bb1, NumberOfTradeableSymbols);
//   
//

//   
//   ArrayInitialize(handle_bb1, INVALID_HANDLE);

//    for (int i = 0; i < NumberOfTradeableSymbols; i++)

//        }
//    }

//    {
//        for (int j = 0; j < 4; j++)
//        {
//            open_symbols[i][j] = 0; // Using double values (1.0, 2.0, 3.0)
//        }
//    }

       // Initialize the start time
    startTime = TimeCurrent();

    // Configure a timer to trigger every 30 seconds
    EventSetTimer(RecordingInterval);

    EnsureFileExists(Filename);

    //int strat_num = 1;

    //##############################################################
    //##############################################################
    
//      NumberOfTradeableSymbols2 = StringSplit(AllSymbolsString2, '|', SymbolArray2);
//    
//    ArrayResize(handle_rsi, NumberOfTradeableSymbols2);
//    ArrayResize(handle_atr, NumberOfTradeableSymbols2);
//

//   ArrayInitialize(handle_rsi, INVALID_HANDLE);
//   
//   //ArrayInitialize(handle_atr, INVALID_HANDLE);
//

//    ArrayResize(open_symbols2, NumberOfTradeableSymbols2);
//    ArrayResize(arrays2, NumberOfTradeableSymbols2);
//    
//    for (int i = 0; i < NumberOfTradeableSymbols2; i++)

//            arrays2[i][j] = 0;
//        }

//        {
//            // Assign values 1, 2, 3 to each array
//            open_symbols2[i][j] = 0; // Using double values (1.0, 2.0, 3.0)
//        }
//    }
    
    //##############################################################
    //##############################################################
    
    AllSymbolsString3 = ReadOrCreateSymbolsFile(AllSymbolsString_file_3, AllSymbolsString_input_3);
    
      
      //CONVERT TradeSymbolsToUse TO THE STRING ARRAY SymbolArray
    //NumberOfTradeableSymbols3 = StringSplit(AllSymbolsString3, '|', SymbolArray3);
    NumberOfTradeableSymbols3 = SplitStringByDelimiters(AllSymbolsString3, SymbolArray3);

    ArrayResize(handle_roc3, NumberOfTradeableSymbols3);
    ArrayResize(handle_atr3, NumberOfTradeableSymbols3);
    
   //ArrayInitialize(handle_roc3, INVALID_HANDLE);
   //ArrayInitialize(handle_atr3, INVALID_HANDLE);
   
    
    ArrayResize(open_symbols3, NumberOfTradeableSymbols3);
    ArrayResize(arrays3, NumberOfTradeableSymbols3);
    
    for (int i = 0; i < NumberOfTradeableSymbols3; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < ARRAY_SIZE; j++)
        {
            arrays3[i][j] = 0;
        }
    }

    for (int i = 0; i < NumberOfTradeableSymbols3; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < 4; j++)
        {
            open_symbols3[i][j] = 0; // Using double values (1.0, 2.0, 3.0)
        }
    }    
    //##############################################################
    //##############################################################
      AllSymbolsString4 = ReadOrCreateSymbolsFile(AllSymbolsString_file_4, AllSymbolsString_input_4);

    ArrayResize(handle_atr4, NumberOfTradeableSymbols4);
    
   ArrayResize(handle_macd4, NumberOfTradeableSymbols4);

    for (int i = 0; i < NumberOfTradeableSymbols4; i++)

            arrays4[i][j] = 0;

    for (int i = 0; i < NumberOfTradeableSymbols4; i++)

            open_symbols4[i][j] = 0; // Using double values (1.0, 2.0, 3.0)
        }

      AllSymbolsString5 = ReadOrCreateSymbolsFile(AllSymbolsString_file_5, AllSymbolsString_input_5);

    NumberOfTradeableSymbols5 = SplitStringByDelimiters(AllSymbolsString5, SymbolArray5);

    ArrayResize(open_symbols5, NumberOfTradeableSymbols5);

    for (int i = 0; i < NumberOfTradeableSymbols5; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < ARRAY_SIZE; j++)
        {
            arrays5[i][j] = 0;
        }
    }
    
    for (int i = 0; i < NumberOfTradeableSymbols5; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < 4; j++)
        {
            // Assign values 1, 2, 3 to each array
            open_symbols5[i][j] = 0; // Using double values (1.0, 2.0, 3.0)
        }
    }    
    //##############################################################
    //##############################################################
//        
//      AllSymbolsString6 = ReadOrCreateSymbolsFile(AllSymbolsString_file_6, AllSymbolsString_input_6);
//      
//    NumberOfTradeableSymbols6 = SplitStringByDelimiters(AllSymbolsString6, SymbolArray6);
//

                          AllSymbolsString8 + "|" + 
                          AllSymbolsString5 + "|" + AllSymbolsString4 + "|" + AllSymbolsString3;
      
    string symbolsRaw[];
   string symbolsUnique[];

   // Split the input string
   int rawCount = StringSplit(symbolString, '|', symbolsRaw);

   if(rawCount == 0)
   {
      Print(" No symbols found in input.");
      return(INIT_FAILED); 
   }

   // Remove duplicates
   for(int i = 0; i < rawCount; i++)
   {
      string s = symbolsRaw[i];
      bool isDuplicate = false;

      for(int j = 0; j < ArraySize(symbolsUnique); j++)
      {
         if(symbolsUnique[j] == s)
         {
            isDuplicate = true;
            break;
         }
      }

      if(!isDuplicate)
      {
         int newSize = ArraySize(symbolsUnique) + 1;
         ArrayResize(symbolsUnique, newSize);
         symbolsUnique[newSize - 1] = s;
      }
   }

   bool symbol_error = false;
   
   // Now check each unique symbol
   for(int i = 0; i < ArraySize(symbolsUnique); i++)
   {
      string symbol = symbolsUnique[i];
   
      if(EnsureSymbolAvailable(symbol))
      {
      }
      else
      {
         Print("Symbol NOT available: ", symbol);
         symbol_error = true;
      }
   }
   
   if(symbol_error)
   {
      return(INIT_FAILED);
   }
   
      
   
//    string server = AccountInfoString(ACCOUNT_SERVER);
//    Print("Connected Server: ", server);
//
//    // Check if the server is in the list
//    for (int i = 0; i < ArraySize(invalidServers); i++)

//        {
//            Print("Invalid Server Detected: ", server);
//            return(INIT_FAILED); ; 
//        }
//    }

    //Print("Server is valid.");    
    
    
   EnsureFileExists(Filename_errors);
   Print("GetLastError ", GetLastError());
   ResetLastError();
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);  // Return success
}

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Expert deinitialization function                                 |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
void OnDeinit(const int reason)
  {
    EventKillTimer();
    Print("WannaBeQuant Strategy Selection EA stopped. version:", version);
     
  }
  

//##################################################################################################################################################################
//##################################################################################################################################################################



// OnTimer function to update the global time every second
void OnTimer() {
    globalTime = TimeCurrent();  
    
    int all_orders = OrdersTotal() + PositionsTotal();
    string commentText = 
        "WannaBeQuant EA:\n" +
        "total orders: " + all_orders + "\n" +
        "drawdown % : " + DoubleToString(drawdown_remaining_daily, 2)+ "\n" +
        "MAX equity DD active: " + equityDD_hit_close+ "\n" +
        "low equity DD active: " + equityDDlow+ "\n" +
        "max Equity: " + DoubleToString(maxEquity, 1) + "\n" +
        "drawdown Threshold: " + DoubleToString(drawdownThreshold2, 1) + "\n" +
        "version: " + DoubleToString(version, 1) + "\n" +
        "is Auto Trading Enabled: " + isAutoTradingEnabled ;

    Comment(commentText);   
    
    
    

   if(record_equity){
      EnsureDatabaseExists("MyDatabase.db");
      RecordEquityToDB(Filename);
   
       // Clean the CSV and get the maximum equity value
       maxEquity = CleanDBAndGetMaxEquity(Filename); //CleanCSVAndGetMaxEquity(Filename);
       if (maxEquity > 0)
       {
           //PrintFormat("The maximum equity value in the last 2 days is: %.2f", maxEquity);
   
           // Get the current equity
           double currentEquity = AccountInfoDouble(ACCOUNT_EQUITY);
   
           // Calculate the 5% threshold
           double drawdownThreshold = maxEquity * drawdownThreshold_percentage;
           drawdownThreshold2 = drawdownThreshold;
           
           double drawdown_remaining_daily = CalculatePercentageSpread(maxEquity, currentEquity);
           
           if (currentEquity < (maxEquity * drawdownThreshold_percentage_OPEN))
           {
               equityDDlow = true;
           }
           else{
               equityDDlow = false;
           }
   
           // Check if the current equity is below the threshold
           if (currentEquity < drawdownThreshold)
           {
               //PrintFormat("Current equity (%.2f) is 5%% less than the maximum equity (%.2f). Take action!", currentEquity, maxEquity);
               equityDD_hit_close = true;
           }
           else{
               equityDD_hit_close = false;
           }
   
       }
       else
       {
           Print("No valid equity data found in the CSV.");
       }
       
       isAutoTradingEnabled = TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_TRADE_ALLOWED) == 1;
       if (isAutoTradingEnabled)
       {
           //Print("AutoTrading is enabled.");
       }
       else
       {
           Print("AutoTrading is disabled.");
       }
     
     
     
       if (CheckTradesWithinLast25Days())
       {
           //Print("There were trades opened or closed within the last 25 days.");
       }
       else
       {
           Print("No trades were opened or closed within the last days.");
           double min = SymbolInfoDouble(CheckTradesWithinLastSymbol, SYMBOL_VOLUME_MIN);
           if(noTradesOpenedInLastDays){
           OpenAndClosePosition(CheckTradesWithinLastSymbol, min);
           }
       }
    }
    
    
    update_counter += RecordingInterval ;
//    update_counter2 += RecordingInterval ;
//    
//    if(update_counter2 >= update_counter_input2){
//      update_counter2 = 0 ;
//         if(crypto_sentiment_strat_1 && TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_CONNECTED)){
////            for(int SymbolLoop = 0; SymbolLoop < NumberOfTradeableSymbols; SymbolLoop++){
////               //count_bars +=1;
////               strategy(SymbolLoop);
////               
////            }
//         }
//    }
         
    update_counter8 += RecordingInterval ;
    if(update_counter8 >= update_counter_input8){
      update_counter8 = 0 ;
         if(crypto_volatility_8 && TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_CONNECTED)){
            for(int SymbolLoop = 0; SymbolLoop < NumberOfTradeableSymbols8; SymbolLoop++){
               crypto_volatility(SymbolLoop);
            }
         }   
    }

    update_counter3 += RecordingInterval ;
    if(update_counter3 >= update_counter_input3){
      update_counter3 = 0 ;
         if(STOCKS_ROC_ATR_strat_3 && TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_CONNECTED)){
            for(int SymbolLoop = 0; SymbolLoop < NumberOfTradeableSymbols3; SymbolLoop++){
               STOCKS_ROC_ATR(SymbolLoop);
            }
         }     
    }
    
    update_counter4 += RecordingInterval ;
    if(update_counter4 >= update_counter_input4){
      update_counter4 = 0 ;
         if(STOCKS_ROC_ATR_strat_4 && TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_CONNECTED)){
            for(int SymbolLoop = 0; SymbolLoop < NumberOfTradeableSymbols4; SymbolLoop++){
               stocks_macd_ema_stoch(SymbolLoop);
            }
         }    
    }
    
    update_counter5 += RecordingInterval ;
    if(update_counter5 >= update_counter_input5){
      update_counter5 = 0 ;
         if(STOCKS_MACD_ATR_strat_5 && TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_CONNECTED)){
            for(int SymbolLoop = 0; SymbolLoop < NumberOfTradeableSymbols5; SymbolLoop++){
               stocks_macd_ATR_stoch5(SymbolLoop);
            }
         }  
    }
    
    //update_counter6 += RecordingInterval ;
    //if(update_counter6 >= update_counter_input6){
    //  update_counter6 = 0 ;
    //     if(crypto_kama_strat_6 && TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_CONNECTED)){
    //        for(int SymbolLoop = 0; SymbolLoop < NumberOfTradeableSymbols6; SymbolLoop++){
    //           crypto_kama_strat(SymbolLoop);
    //        }
    //     }  
    //}    
    
//    update_counter7 += RecordingInterval ;
//    if(update_counter7 >= update_counter_input7){
//      update_counter7 = 0 ;
//         if(STOCKS_volatility_atr_7 && TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_CONNECTED)){
//            for(int SymbolLoop = 0; SymbolLoop < NumberOfTradeableSymbols7; SymbolLoop++){
//               STOCKS_volatility_atr(SymbolLoop);
//            }
//         }   
//    }       
//             
    update_counter11 += RecordingInterval ;
    if(update_counter11 >= update_counter_input11){
      update_counter11 = 0 ;
         if(crypto_turtle_11 && TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_CONNECTED)){
            for(int SymbolLoop = 0; SymbolLoop < NumberOfTradeableSymbols11; SymbolLoop++){
               crypto_turtle_strat_11(SymbolLoop);
            }
         }  
    }      
    
    //update_counter12 += RecordingInterval ;
    //if(update_counter12 >= update_counter_input12){
    //  update_counter12 = 0 ;
    //     if(STOCKS_MACD_ATR_strat_12 && TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_CONNECTED)){
    //        for(int SymbolLoop = 0; SymbolLoop < NumberOfTradeableSymbols12; SymbolLoop++){
    //           stocks_macd_ATR_stoch12(SymbolLoop);
    //        }
    //     }     
    //}    
    
    update_counter13 += RecordingInterval ;
    if(update_counter13 >= update_counter_input13){
      update_counter13 = 0 ;
         if(crypto_strat_13_bool && TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_CONNECTED)){
            for(int SymbolLoop = 0; SymbolLoop < NumberOfTradeableSymbols13; SymbolLoop++){
               crypto_strat_13(SymbolLoop);
            }
         } 
    }              
   
    if(update_counter >= update_counter_input){
      update_counter = 0 ;
      
          // Check if the terminal is connected
          if (!TerminalInfoInteger(TERMINAL_CONNECTED))
          {
              if(!ignor_terminal_error){Print("Terminal is not connected.");}
              return; // Server is OFF
          }
      
                                       
         if(MQLInfoInteger(MQL_TESTER)) //Only run in live account
         {
            MqlDateTime currentDateTime;
            TimeCurrent(currentDateTime);
            
            if(currentDateTime.hour != PreviousHourlyTasksRun)
            {
               int currentArraySize = ArraySize(EquityHistoryArray);
               ArrayResize(EquityHistoryArray, currentArraySize + 1);  
               EquityHistoryArray[currentArraySize] = AccountInfoDouble(ACCOUNT_EQUITY);
            }
            
            PreviousHourlyTasksRun = currentDateTime.hour;
         }
         
   }


    
}

double CalculateChoppinessIndex13(string symbol)
{
    // Ensure enough bars are available
    if (Bars(symbol, ci_timeframe13) < length13 + 1) return -1;

    // Initialize variables
    double sumATR = 0;
    double highArray[], lowArray[], closeArray[];

    // Copy price data
    if (CopyHigh(symbol, ci_timeframe13, 0, length13 + 1, highArray) < length13 + 1) return -1;
    if (CopyLow(symbol, ci_timeframe13, 0, length13 + 1, lowArray) < length13 + 1) return -1;
    if (CopyClose(symbol, ci_timeframe13, 0, length13 + 1, closeArray) < length13 + 1) return -1;

    // Calculate ATR(1) manually
    for (int i = 0; i < length13; i++) // Loop only up to length-1 to avoid out-of-range
    {
        double tr = MathMax(highArray[i] - lowArray[i], 
                            MathMax(fabs(highArray[i] - closeArray[i+1]), 
                                    fabs(lowArray[i] - closeArray[i+1])));
        sumATR += tr;
    }

    // Get highest high and lowest low over 'length' period
    int highestIndex = iHighest(symbol, ci_timeframe13, MODE_HIGH, length13, 0);
    int lowestIndex = iLowest(symbol, ci_timeframe13, MODE_LOW, length13, 0);

    double highestHigh = iHigh(symbol, ci_timeframe13, highestIndex);
    double lowestLow = iLow(symbol, ci_timeframe13, lowestIndex);

    // Ensure valid denominator
    if (highestHigh - lowestLow == 0) return -1;

    // Compute Choppiness Index formula
    double ci = 100 * (MathLog10(sumATR / (highestHigh - lowestLow)) / MathLog10(length13));

    return ci;
}


void crypto_strat_13(int SymbolLoop){
   ResetLastError();
   string symbol = SymbolArray13[SymbolLoop];

   int strat_num = 13;
   if(!IsMarketOpen(symbol)){return;};
   int uniqueOriginalIDCount = 0;
   
   
   if(!backtest_active){
   bool selected = SymbolSelect(symbol, true);
   if(!selected){Print("symbol not in market watch? ", symbol); return;};
   }
   
   double openPrices[];
   int totalOpenPrices = CopyOpen(symbol, PERIOD_D1, 0, 50, openPrices);
   
   if (totalOpenPrices < 50)
   {
       PrintFormat("Insufficient historical open prices: Only %d available for %s on timeframe %s.",
                   totalOpenPrices, symbol, EnumToString(PERIOD_D1));
       return;
   }
   
    update_open_symbol13(SymbolLoop);
    if (open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][1] != 1)
    {
        //Print(symbol," symbol is not trading righ now ");
        return;
    }
    
   if (handle_bb13[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      ResetLastError();
      handle_bb13[SymbolLoop] = iBands(SymbolArray13[SymbolLoop], bb_timeframe13, bands_period13, 0, BB_deveation13, BB_PRICE13);
      if (handle_bb13[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         int err = GetLastError();
         string msg = "Failed to create RSI handle for " + symbol + " (error: " + IntegerToString(err) + ")";
         if (err == 4302)
            msg += " - Symbol needs to be added to Market Watch.";
         Print(msg);
         return;
      }
   }
 
 
    double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol,SYMBOL_BID);
   double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol,SYMBOL_ASK);
   double spreadPercent = ((ask-bid) / ask) * 100.0;

   double higharray[], lowarray[], closearray[];
   int count = ATRinput13 + 1;
   if (CopyHigh(symbol, atr_timeframe13, 0, count, higharray) != count ||
       CopyLow(symbol, atr_timeframe13, 0, count, lowarray) != count ||
       CopyClose(symbol, atr_timeframe13, 0, count, closearray) != count)
   {
      Print("Failed to load price data.");
      return;
   }

   ArraySetAsSeries(higharray, true);
   ArraySetAsSeries(lowarray, true);
   ArraySetAsSeries(closearray, true);

   // --- Calculate custom ATR for current bar only ---
   double atr_value = GetCustomATR(higharray, lowarray, closearray, ATRinput13);

   //double atr_buffer[];
   //CopyBuffer(handle_atr13[SymbolLoop], 0, 0, 1, atr_buffer);
   //double atr_value = atr_buffer[0];
   
   double upperBand[], middleBand[], lowerBand[];
   int barsToGet = 1; // Retrieve the most recent value
   int barIndex = 0; // For the current bar
   
   // Copy the Upper Band value
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_bb13[SymbolLoop], 0, barIndex, barsToGet, upperBand) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve upper band: ", GetLastError());
   }
   
   // Copy the Middle Band value
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_bb13[SymbolLoop], 1, barIndex, barsToGet, middleBand) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve middle band: ", GetLastError());
   }
   
   // Copy the Lower Band value
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_bb13[SymbolLoop], 2, barIndex, barsToGet, lowerBand) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve lower band: ", GetLastError());
   }
   
   double bbw = ((upperBand[0] - lowerBand[0]) / middleBand[0]) * 100 ;
   
 
      
   if (handle_ichi13[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      ResetLastError();
      handle_ichi13[SymbolLoop] = iIchimoku(SymbolArray13[SymbolLoop], ichi_period13, tenkan_sen13, kijun_sen13, senkou_span_b13);
      if (handle_ichi13[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         int err = GetLastError();
         string msg = "Failed to create RSI handle for " + symbol + " (error: " + IntegerToString(err) + ")";
         if (err == 4302)
            msg += " - Symbol needs to be added to Market Watch.";
         Print(msg);
         return;
      }
   }
   if (handle_adx13[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      ResetLastError();
      handle_adx13[SymbolLoop] = iADX(SymbolArray13[SymbolLoop], adx_timeframe13, ADXlength13);
      if (handle_adx13[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         int err = GetLastError();
         string msg = "Failed to create RSI handle for " + symbol + " (error: " + IntegerToString(err) + ")";
         if (err == 4302)
            msg += " - Symbol needs to be added to Market Watch.";
         Print(msg);
         return;
      }
   }   
   
 

   double tenkan_sen1[], kijun_sen1[], senkou_span_a1[], senkou_span_b1[];

   // Copy the latest values of Ichimoku indicator
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_ichi13[SymbolLoop], 0, 0, 1, tenkan_sen1) <= 0 ||
       CopyBuffer(handle_ichi13[SymbolLoop], 1, 0, 1, kijun_sen1) <= 0 ||
       CopyBuffer(handle_ichi13[SymbolLoop], 2, 0, 1, senkou_span_a1) <= 0 ||
       CopyBuffer(handle_ichi13[SymbolLoop], 3, 0, 1, senkou_span_b1) <= 0)
   {
      Print("Failed to copy Ichimoku indicator buffers");
      return;
   }

   int signal_ichi = 0;
   if (tenkan_sen1[0] > kijun_sen1[0] && senkou_span_a1[0] > senkou_span_b1[0])
      signal_ichi = 1;

   if (tenkan_sen1[0] < kijun_sen1[0] && senkou_span_a1[0] < senkou_span_b1[0])
      signal_ichi = -1;

   
   double adx_buffer[];
   CopyBuffer(handle_adx13[SymbolLoop], 0, 0, 1, adx_buffer);
   double adx_value = adx_buffer[0];
   
   
   double ci = CalculateChoppinessIndex13(symbol);
   if (ci == -1) Print(ci," ci bugged "); // Exit if calculation fails
    

      // Print all values for debugging
   //Print("CI: ", ci, " | Open: ", open, " | ADX: ", adx_value, " | BBW: ", bbw, " | signal_ichi: ", signal_ichi);
   
   bool long_now = false;
   if(ci<ci_thresh13 && signal_ichi==1 && adx_value>adx_value_thresh13  && bbw<bbw_thresh13 ){
      long_now = true;
   }
   
   bool short_now = false;
   if(ci<ci_thresh13 && signal_ichi==-1 && adx_value>adx_value_thresh13  && bbw<bbw_thresh13 ){
      short_now = true;
   }
       


    ulong positionTicket = 0 ;
    string string_STRAT_NUM = "13";
    string tableName = "Long" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
    int ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
    PositionData position;
    ResetPositionData(position);
    if(arrays13[SymbolLoop][0] != -1){
    
     if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
       else{return;};
      if (position.PositionID != 0 )
      {
         arrays13[SymbolLoop][0] = 1 ;
         if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID) ) 
         {
            //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
         }
         else
         {
            if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
            int arraydelete[1];
            arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
            Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
            DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
            ResetPositionData(position);
            }
         }
      }
      else
      {
         arrays13[SymbolLoop][0] = -1 ;
      }
   }
   
   string side = "long"; 
   double TP = ask + (atr_value*tp_atr_multi13); 
   double SL = ask - (atr_value*sl_atr_multi13);  
   double TrailTP = 0; 
   double TrailThresh = 0;  
   string ExpiryDate = globalTime;
   double nums[20];
   for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
       nums[i] = 0;  
   }
   if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh13 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && long_now  ){
      uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray13);
      if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades13){
         trade_entry(comment13_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat13OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L13, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
         arrays13[SymbolLoop][0] = 1 ;
      }
   }
    if(position.PositionID!=0){
      if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID))  // Select the position by ticket
      {
         datetime open_time = (datetime)PositionGetInteger(POSITION_TIME);
         
         int elapsedTime = (int)(globalTime - open_time);  // Calculate elapsed time in seconds
         int remainingTime = countdownDuration13 - elapsedTime;          // Calculate remaining time
      
         if(position.PositionID!=0 && remainingTime<=0  ){
            Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
            CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
         }
         
      }
   }
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid > position.TP  && !long_now){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && ask < position.SL ){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }      
   
   
    positionTicket = 0 ;
    string_STRAT_NUM = "13";
    tableName = "Short" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
    ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
    ResetPositionData(position);
    if(arrays13[SymbolLoop][1] != -1){
    
       if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
          else{return;};
         if (position.PositionID != 0)
         {
            arrays13[SymbolLoop][1] = 1;
            if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID)) 
            {
               //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
            }
            else
            {
               if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
               int arraydelete[1];
               arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
               Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
               DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
               ResetPositionData(position);
               }
            }
         }
         else
         {
            arrays13[SymbolLoop][1] = -1;
         }
     }

   side = "short"; 
   TP = bid - (atr_value*tp_atr_multi13); 
   SL = bid + (atr_value*sl_atr_multi13);  
   TrailTP = 0; 
   TrailThresh = 0;  
   ExpiryDate = globalTime;
   for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
       nums[i] = 0;  
   }
   if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh13 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && short_now){
      uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray13);
      if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades13){
         trade_entry(comment13_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat13OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L13, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
         arrays13[SymbolLoop][1] = 1 ;
      }
   }
   
    if(position.PositionID!=0){
      if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID))  // Select the position by ticket
      {
         datetime open_time = (datetime)PositionGetInteger(POSITION_TIME);
         
         int elapsedTime = (int)(globalTime - open_time);  // Calculate elapsed time in seconds
         int remainingTime = countdownDuration13 - elapsedTime;          // Calculate remaining time
      
         if(position.PositionID!=0 && remainingTime<=0  ){
            Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
            CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
         }
         
      }
   }
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && ask < position.TP && !short_now){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }     
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid > position.SL ){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }   
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }      

   
   
   if(!backtest_active){
   LogErrorToCSV();
   }
   
}
