double GetRecentHighLow(string symbol, ENUM_TIMEFRAMES timeframe, int bars_count, double &recent_high, double &recent_low)
{
   recent_high = -DBL_MAX; // Initialize to the smallest possible value
   recent_low  = DBL_MAX;  // Initialize to the largest possible value

   for(int i = 0; i < bars_count; i++)
   {
      double high = iHigh(symbol, timeframe, i+1);
      double low  = iLow(symbol, timeframe, i+1);

      if(high > recent_high) recent_high = high;
      if(low < recent_low) recent_low = low;
   }
   return 0;
}




double CalculateChoppinessIndex11(string symbol)
{
    // Ensure enough bars are available
    if (Bars(symbol, ci_timeframe11) < length11 + 1) return -1;

    // Initialize variables
    double sumATR = 0;
    double highArray[], lowArray[], closeArray[];

    // Copy price data
    if (CopyHigh(symbol, ci_timeframe11, 0, length11 + 1, highArray) < length11 + 1) return -1;
    if (CopyLow(symbol, ci_timeframe11, 0, length11 + 1, lowArray) < length11 + 1) return -1;
    if (CopyClose(symbol, ci_timeframe11, 0, length11 + 1, closeArray) < length11 + 1) return -1;

    // Calculate ATR(1) manually
    for (int i = 0; i < length11; i++) // Loop only up to length-1 to avoid out-of-range
    {
        double tr = MathMax(highArray[i] - lowArray[i], 
                            MathMax(fabs(highArray[i] - closeArray[i+1]), 
                                    fabs(lowArray[i] - closeArray[i+1])));
        sumATR += tr;
    }

    // Get highest high and lowest low over 'length' period
    int highestIndex = iHighest(symbol, ci_timeframe11, MODE_HIGH, length11, 0);
    int lowestIndex = iLowest(symbol, ci_timeframe11, MODE_LOW, length11, 0);

    double highestHigh = iHigh(symbol, ci_timeframe11, highestIndex);
    double lowestLow = iLow(symbol, ci_timeframe11, lowestIndex);

    // Ensure valid denominator
    if (highestHigh - lowestLow == 0) return -1;

    // Compute Choppiness Index formula
    double ci = 100 * (MathLog10(sumATR / (highestHigh - lowestLow)) / MathLog10(length11));

    return ci;
}



void crypto_turtle_strat_11(int SymbolLoop){
   ResetLastError();
   string symbol = SymbolArray11[SymbolLoop];
   string symbol2 = SymbolArray11[SymbolLoop];
   string symbol_without_dot = symbol2.Replace(".", "");

   int strat_num = 11;
   if(!IsMarketOpen(symbol)){return;};
   int uniqueOriginalIDCount = 0;
   
   
   if(!backtest_active){
   bool selected = SymbolSelect(symbol, true);
   if(!selected){Print("symbol not in market watch? ", symbol); return;};
   }
   
   double openPrices[];
   int totalOpenPrices = CopyOpen(symbol, PERIOD_D1, 0, 50, openPrices);
   
   if (totalOpenPrices < 50)
   {
       PrintFormat("Insufficient historical open prices: Only %d available for %s on timeframe %s.",
                   totalOpenPrices, symbol, EnumToString(PERIOD_D1));
       return;
   }
   
    update_open_symbol11(SymbolLoop);
    if (open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][1] != 1)
    {
        //Print(symbol," symbol is not trading righ now ");
        return;
    }
    
   double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol,SYMBOL_BID);
   double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol,SYMBOL_ASK);
   double spreadPercent = ((ask-bid) / ask) * 100.0;
   
   double higharray[], lowarray[], closearray[];
   int count = ATRinput11 + 1;
   if (CopyHigh(symbol, atr_timeframe11, 0, count, higharray) != count ||
       CopyLow(symbol, atr_timeframe11, 0, count, lowarray) != count ||
       CopyClose(symbol, atr_timeframe11, 0, count, closearray) != count)
   {
      Print("Failed to load price data.");
      return;
   }

   ArraySetAsSeries(higharray, true);
   ArraySetAsSeries(lowarray, true);
   ArraySetAsSeries(closearray, true);

   // --- Calculate custom ATR for current bar only ---
   double atr_value = GetCustomATR(higharray, lowarray, closearray, ATRinput11);
   
   double upperBand[], middleBand[], lowerBand[];
   int barsToGet = 1; // Retrieve the most recent value
   int barIndex = 0; // For the current bar
   
   if (handle_adx11[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      ResetLastError();
      handle_adx11[SymbolLoop] = iADX(SymbolArray11[SymbolLoop], adx_timeframe11, ADXlength11);
      if (handle_adx11[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         int err = GetLastError();
         string msg = "Failed to create RSI handle for " + symbol + " (error: " + IntegerToString(err) + ")";
         if (err == 4302)
            msg += " - Symbol needs to be added to Market Watch.";
         Print(msg);
         return;
      }
   }
         // --- Create handle only if needed ---
   if (handle_bb11[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      ResetLastError();
      handle_bb11[SymbolLoop] = iBands(SymbolArray11[SymbolLoop], bb_timeframe11, bands_period11, 0, BB_deveation11, BB_PRICE11);
      if (handle_bb11[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         int err = GetLastError();
         string msg = "Failed to create RSI handle for " + symbol + " (error: " + IntegerToString(err) + ")";
         if (err == 4302)
            msg += " - Symbol needs to be added to Market Watch.";
         Print(msg);
         return;
      }
   }
   
      
   // Copy the Upper Band value
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_bb11[SymbolLoop], 0, barIndex, barsToGet, upperBand) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve upper band: ", GetLastError());
   }
   
   // Copy the Middle Band value
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_bb11[SymbolLoop], 1, barIndex, barsToGet, middleBand) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve middle band: ", GetLastError());
   }
   
   // Copy the Lower Band value
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_bb11[SymbolLoop], 2, barIndex, barsToGet, lowerBand) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve lower band: ", GetLastError());
   }
   
   double bbw = ((upperBand[0] - lowerBand[0]) / middleBand[0]) * 100 ;
   
   double high, low;
   GetRecentHighLow(symbol, hl_timeframe11 , hl_length11, high, low);

   double adx_buffer[];
   CopyBuffer(handle_adx11[SymbolLoop], 0, 0, 1, adx_buffer);
   double adx_value = adx_buffer[0];
   
   
   double ci = CalculateChoppinessIndex11(symbol);
   if (ci == -1) Print(ci," ci bugged "); // Exit if calculation fails

   //Print("CI: ", ci, " | Open: ", open, " | ADX: ", adx_value, " | BBW: ", bbw, " | high: ", high, " | low: ", low );
   
   bool long_now = false;
   if(ci<ci_thresh11 && bid > high && adx_value>adx_value_thresh11  && bbw<bbw_thresh11 ){
      long_now = true;
   }
   
   bool short_now = false;
   if(ci<ci_thresh11 && ask < low && adx_value>adx_value_thresh11  && bbw<bbw_thresh11 ){
      short_now = true;
   }



    ulong positionTicket = 0 ;
    string string_STRAT_NUM = "11";
    string tableName = "Long" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
    int ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
    PositionData position;
    ResetPositionData(position);
    if(arrays11[SymbolLoop][0] != -1){
    
    if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
       else{return;};
      if (position.PositionID != 0)
      {
         arrays11[SymbolLoop][0] = 1;
         if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID)) 
         {
            //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
         }
         else
         {
            if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
            int arraydelete[1];
            arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
            Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
            DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
            ResetPositionData(position);
            }
         }
      }
      else
      {
         arrays11[SymbolLoop][0] = -1;
      }
   }
   
   string side = "long"; 
   double TP = ask + (atr_value*tp_atr_multi11); 
   double SL = ask - (atr_value*sl_atr_multi11);  
   double TrailTP = 0; 
   double TrailThresh = 0;  
   string ExpiryDate = globalTime;
   double nums[20];
   for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
       nums[i] = 0;  
   }
   if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh11 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && long_now  ){
      uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray11);
      if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades11){
         trade_entry(comment11_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat11OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L11, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
         arrays11[SymbolLoop][0] = 1 ;
      }
   }
    if(position.PositionID!=0){
      if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID))  // Select the position by ticket
      {
         datetime open_time = (datetime)PositionGetInteger(POSITION_TIME);
         
         int elapsedTime = (int)(globalTime - open_time);  // Calculate elapsed time in seconds
         int remainingTime = countdownDuration11 - elapsedTime;          // Calculate remaining time
      
         if(position.PositionID!=0 && remainingTime<=0  ){
            Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
            CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
         }
         
      }
   }
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid > position.TP  && !long_now){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && ask < position.SL ){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }      
   
   
    positionTicket = 0 ;
    string_STRAT_NUM = "11";
    tableName = "Short" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
    ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
    ResetPositionData(position);
    if(arrays11[SymbolLoop][1] != -1){
    
    if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
       else{return;};
      if (position.PositionID != 0)
      {
         arrays11[SymbolLoop][1] = 1 ;
         if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID)) 
         {
            //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
         }
         else
         {
            if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
            int arraydelete[1];
            arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
            Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
            DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
            ResetPositionData(position);
            }
         }
      }
      else
      {
         arrays11[SymbolLoop][1] = -1 ;
      }
   }

   side = "short"; 
   TP = bid - (atr_value*tp_atr_multi11); 
   SL = bid + (atr_value*sl_atr_multi11);  
   TrailTP = 0; 
   TrailThresh = 0;  
   ExpiryDate = globalTime;
   for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
       nums[i] = 0;  
   }
   if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh11 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && short_now){
      uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray11);
      if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades11){
         trade_entry(comment11_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat11OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L11, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
         arrays11[SymbolLoop][1] = 1 ;
      }
   }
    if(position.PositionID!=0){
      if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID))  // Select the position by ticket
      {
         datetime open_time = (datetime)PositionGetInteger(POSITION_TIME);
         
         int elapsedTime = (int)(globalTime - open_time);  // Calculate elapsed time in seconds
         int remainingTime = countdownDuration11 - elapsedTime;          // Calculate remaining time
      
         if(position.PositionID!=0 && remainingTime<=0  ){
            Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
            CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
         }
         
      }
   }
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && ask < position.TP && !short_now){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }     
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid > position.SL ){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }   
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }      
   LogErrorToCSV();
   
   
   
   
   
   if(!backtest_active){
   LogErrorToCSV();
   }
   
}   
   
   
   

void crypto_volatility(int SymbolLoop){
   ResetLastError();
   string symbol = SymbolArray8[SymbolLoop];
   int strat_num = 8;
   if(!IsMarketOpen(symbol)){return;};
   int uniqueOriginalIDCount = 0 ;
   
   
   if(!backtest_active){
   bool selected = SymbolSelect(symbol, true);
   if(!selected){Print("symbol not in market watch? ", symbol); return;};
   }
   
   double openPrices[];
   int totalOpenPrices = CopyOpen(symbol, PERIOD_D1, 0, 50, openPrices);
   
   if (totalOpenPrices < 50)
   {
       PrintFormat("Insufficient historical open prices: Only %d available for %s on timeframe %s.",
                   totalOpenPrices, symbol, EnumToString(PERIOD_D1));
       return;
   }
    update_open_symbol8(SymbolLoop);
    if (open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][1] != 1)
    {
        return;
    }

   datetime currentBarTime = iTime(Symbol(), Period(), 0);
   double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol,SYMBOL_BID);
   double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol,SYMBOL_ASK);
   double spreadPercent = ((ask-bid) / ask) * 100.0;
    double averages[];  // Array to store 10 averages
    ArrayResize(averages, smoothing_leng_bands8);
    // Calculate 10 averages
    for (int i = 0; i < smoothing_leng_bands8; i++)
    {
          int highestIndex = iHighest(symbol, PERIOD_H1, MODE_HIGH, average_PERIOD8, i + 1); // Skip the current bar (shift=1)
          double highestValue = iHigh(symbol, PERIOD_H1, highestIndex);
      
          // Calculate the lowest low
          int lowestIndex = iLowest(symbol, PERIOD_H1, MODE_LOW, average_PERIOD8, i + 1); // Skip the current bar (shift=1)
          double lowestValue = iLow(symbol, PERIOD_H1, lowestIndex);

        // Calculate the average and store it in the array
        averages[i] = (highestValue + lowestValue) / 2;
    }

    // Calculate the Moving Average from the 10 averages
    double sum = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < smoothing_leng_bands8; i++)
    {
        sum += averages[i];
    }
    double ma_value = sum / smoothing_leng_bands8;
    
    double band_high_1 = (envelope_1_pct > 0) ? (ma_value * (1 + envelope_1_pct)) : 0; // Use 0 or EMPTY_VALUE instead of `na`
    double band_high_2 = (envelope_2_pct > 0) ? (ma_value * (1 + envelope_2_pct)) : 0;
    double band_high_3 = (envelope_3_pct > 0) ? (ma_value * (1 + envelope_3_pct)) : 0;
    //double band_high_4 = (envelope_4_pct > 0) ? (ma_value * (1 + envelope_4_pct)) : 0;
    //double band_high_5 = (envelope_5_pct > 0) ? (ma_value * (1 + envelope_5_pct)) : 0;
    
    double band_low_1 = (envelope_1_pct > 0) ? (ma_value * (1 - envelope_1_pct)) : 0;
    double band_low_2 = (envelope_2_pct > 0) ? (ma_value * (1 - envelope_2_pct)) : 0;
    double band_low_3 = (envelope_3_pct > 0) ? (ma_value * (1 - envelope_3_pct)) : 0;
    //double band_low_4 = (envelope_4_pct > 0) ? (ma_value * (1 - envelope_4_pct)) : 0;
    //double band_low_5 = (envelope_5_pct > 0) ? (ma_value * (1 - envelope_5_pct)) : 0;
    
    
    ulong positionTicket = 0 ;
    string string_STRAT_NUM = "8";
    string tableName = "Long" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
    int ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
    PositionData position;
    ResetPositionData(position);
    if(arrays8[SymbolLoop][0] != -1){
    if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
    else{return;};
   if (position.PositionID != 0)
   {
      arrays8[SymbolLoop][0] = 1 ;
      // Check if PositionID is valid (≠ 0) and if it's still active
      if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID)) 
      {
         //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
      }
      else
      {
         if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
         int arraydelete[1];
         arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
         Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
         DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
         ResetPositionData(position);
         }
      }
   }
   else
   {
      arrays8[SymbolLoop][0] = -1 ;
   }
   }
   
    
   if(envelope_1_pct > 0){
   
         string side = "long"; 
         double TP = 0; 
         double SL = ask*(1-stop_loss_pct8);  
         double TrailTP = 0; 
         double TrailThresh = 0;  
         string ExpiryDate = globalTime;
         double nums[20];
         for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
             nums[i] = 0;  
         }
         if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh8 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && band_low_1>=ask ){
            uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray8);
            if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades8){
               trade_entry(comment8_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat8OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L8, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
               arrays8[SymbolLoop][0] = 1 ;
            }
         } 
         
   
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && ask <= position.SL ){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid > ma_value ){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }   
      
       positionTicket = 0 ;
       string_STRAT_NUM = "8";
       tableName = "Short" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
       ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
       ResetPositionData(position);
       if(arrays8[SymbolLoop][1] != -1){
    
       if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
       else{return;};
         if (position.PositionID != 0)
         {
            arrays8[SymbolLoop][1] = 1 ;
            if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID)) 
            {
               //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
            }
            else
            {
               if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
               int arraydelete[1];
               arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
               Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
               DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
               ResetPositionData(position);
               }
            }
         }
         else
         {
            arrays8[SymbolLoop][1] = -1 ;
         }
      }
      
      side = "short"; 
      TP = 0; 
      SL = bid*(1+stop_loss_pct8);  
      TrailTP = 0; 
      TrailThresh = 0;  
      ExpiryDate = globalTime;
      for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
          nums[i] = 0;  
      }
      if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh8 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && band_high_1<=bid ){
         uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray8);
         if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades8){
            trade_entry(comment8_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat8OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L8, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
            arrays8[SymbolLoop][1] = 1 ;
         }
      } 

   if(position.PositionID!=0 && ask < ma_value ){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }     
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid >= position.SL ){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }  
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }   
      
   }
 
  //########################################################################################################################
  //########################################################################################################################

   symbol = SymbolArray9[SymbolLoop];

    positionTicket = 0 ;
    string_STRAT_NUM = "9";
    tableName = "Long" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
    ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
    ResetPositionData(position);
    if(arrays8[SymbolLoop][2] != -1){
    
    if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
       else{return;};
      if (position.PositionID != 0)
      {
         arrays8[SymbolLoop][2] = 1 ;
         if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID)) 
         {
            //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
         }
         else
         {
            if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
            int arraydelete[1];
            arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
            Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
            DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
            ResetPositionData(position);
            }
         }
      }
      else
      {
         arrays8[SymbolLoop][2] = -1 ;
      }
   }

   if(envelope_2_pct > 0){
   
         string side = "long"; 
         double TP = 0; 
         double SL = ask*(1-stop_loss_pct8);  
         double TrailTP = 0; 
         double TrailThresh = 0;  
         string ExpiryDate = globalTime;
         double nums[20];
         for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
             nums[i] = 0;  
         }
         if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh8 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && band_low_2>=ask){
            uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray8);
            if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades8){
               trade_entry(comment8_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat8OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L8, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
               arrays8[SymbolLoop][2] = 1 ;
            }
         } 
         
 
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && ask <= position.SL ){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid > ma_value ){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }      
   
       positionTicket = 0 ;
       string_STRAT_NUM = "9";
       tableName = "Short" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
       ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
       ResetPositionData(position);
       if(arrays8[SymbolLoop][3] != -1){
    
       if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
       else{return;};
         if (position.PositionID != 0)
         {
            arrays8[SymbolLoop][3] = 1 ;
            if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID)) 
            {
               //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
            }
            else
            {
               if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
               int arraydelete[1];
               arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
               Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
               DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
               ResetPositionData(position);
               }
            }
         }
         else
         {
            arrays8[SymbolLoop][3] = -1 ;
         }
      }

      
      side = "short"; 
      TP = 0; 
      SL = bid*(1+stop_loss_pct8);  
      TrailTP = 0; 
      TrailThresh = 0;  
      ExpiryDate = globalTime;
      for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
          nums[i] = 0;  
      }
      if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh8 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && band_high_2<=bid ){
         uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray8);
         if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades8){
            trade_entry(comment8_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat8OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L8, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
            arrays8[SymbolLoop][3] = 1 ;
         }
      } 
      
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && ask < ma_value ){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }     
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid >= position.SL ){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }   
   }   
   
   
  //########################################################################################################################
  //########################################################################################################################

   symbol = SymbolArray10[SymbolLoop];

   
    positionTicket = 0 ;
    string_STRAT_NUM = "10";
    tableName = "Long" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
    ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
    ResetPositionData(position);
    if(arrays8[SymbolLoop][4] != -1){
       
    if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
       else{return;};
      if (position.PositionID != 0)
      {
         arrays8[SymbolLoop][4] = 1 ;
         if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID)) 
         {
            //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
         }
         else
         {
            if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
            int arraydelete[1];
            arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
            Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
            DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
            ResetPositionData(position);
            }
         }
      }
      else
      {
         arrays8[SymbolLoop][4] = -1 ;
      }
   }


   if(envelope_3_pct > 0){
   
      string side = "long"; 
      double TP = 0; 
      double SL = ask*(1-stop_loss_pct8);  
      double TrailTP = 0; 
      double TrailThresh = 0;  
      string ExpiryDate = globalTime;
      double nums[20];
      for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
          nums[i] = 0;  
      }
      if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh8 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && band_low_3>=ask){
         uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray8);
         if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades8){
            trade_entry(comment8_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat8OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L8, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
            arrays8[SymbolLoop][4] = 1 ;
         } 
      }
 
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && ask <= position.SL ){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid > ma_value ){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }      
   
    positionTicket = 0 ;
    string_STRAT_NUM = "10";
    tableName = "Short" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
    ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
    ResetPositionData(position);
    if(arrays8[SymbolLoop][5] != -1){
    
    if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
       else{return;};
      if (position.PositionID != 0)
      {
         arrays8[SymbolLoop][5] = 1 ;
         if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID)) 
         {
            //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
         }
         else
         {
            if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
            int arraydelete[1];
            arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
            Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
            DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
            ResetPositionData(position);
            }
         }
      }
      else
      {
         arrays8[SymbolLoop][5] = -1 ;
      }
   }
      
   
   side = "short"; 
   TP = 0; 
   SL = bid*(1+stop_loss_pct8);  
   TrailTP = 0; 
   TrailThresh = 0;  
   ExpiryDate = globalTime;
   for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
       nums[i] = 0;  
   }
   if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh8 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && band_high_3<=bid ){
      uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray8);
      if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades8){
         trade_entry(comment8_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat8OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L8, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
         arrays8[SymbolLoop][5] = 1 ;
      }
   }

      if(position.PositionID!=0 && ask < ma_value ){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }     
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid >= position.SL ){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }
      if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
         Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
         CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
      }    
   }   
  
   if(!backtest_active){
   LogErrorToCSV();
   }
}

void stocks_macd_ATR_stoch5(int SymbolLoop){
   ResetLastError();
   string symbol = SymbolArray5[SymbolLoop];
   int strat_num = 5;
   if(!IsMarketOpen(symbol)){return;};
   int uniqueOriginalIDCount = 0 ;
   
   bool selected = SymbolSelect(symbol, true);
   if(!selected){Print("symbol not in market watch? ", symbol); return;};

   double openPrices[];
   int totalOpenPrices = CopyOpen(symbol, PERIOD_D1, 0, 50, openPrices);
   
   if (totalOpenPrices < 50)
   {
       PrintFormat("Insufficient historical open prices: Only %d available for %s on timeframe %s.",
                   totalOpenPrices, symbol, EnumToString(PERIOD_D1));
       return;
   }


    update_open_symbol5(SymbolLoop);
    if (open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][1] != 1)
    {
        return;
    }
    
    ulong positionTicket = 0 ;
    string string_STRAT_NUM = "5";
    string tableName = "Long" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
    int ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
    PositionData position;
    ResetPositionData(position);
    if(arrays5[SymbolLoop][0] != -1){
    
    if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
       else{return;};
      if (position.PositionID != 0)
      {
         arrays5[SymbolLoop][0] = 1 ;
         if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID)) 
         {
            //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
         }
         else
         {
            if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
            int arraydelete[1];
            arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
            Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
            DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
            ResetPositionData(position);
            }
         }
      }
      else
      {
         arrays5[SymbolLoop][0] = -1 ;
      }
   }      

   double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol,SYMBOL_BID);
   double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol,SYMBOL_ASK);
   double spreadPercent = ((ask-bid) / ask) * 100.0;
   double open = iOpen(symbol,indicator5_timeframe_1D,0);
   double close = iClose(symbol,indicator5_timeframe_1D,1);
   double high = iHigh(symbol,indicator5_timeframe_1D,2);
   double low = iLow(symbol,indicator5_timeframe_1D,2);

   double higharray[], lowarray[], closearray[];
   int count = ATRinput5 + 1;
   if (CopyHigh(symbol, ATRPeriod5, 0, count, higharray) != count ||
       CopyLow(symbol, ATRPeriod5, 0, count, lowarray) != count ||
       CopyClose(symbol, ATRPeriod5, 0, count, closearray) != count)
   {
      Print("Failed to load price data.");
      return;
   }

   ArraySetAsSeries(higharray, true);
   ArraySetAsSeries(lowarray, true);
   ArraySetAsSeries(closearray, true);

   // --- Calculate custom ATR for current bar only ---
   double atr_value = GetCustomATR(higharray, lowarray, closearray, ATRinput5);

   int startBarIndex = 0; // Starting from the most recent bar (index 0)
   int lowestIndex = iLowest(symbol, indicator5_timeframe_1D, MODE_LOW, barsToCheck, startBarIndex);
   double lowestLow = iLow(symbol, indicator5_timeframe_1D, lowestIndex);
   double diff_sl_tp = ask - lowestLow;
   double sl = lowestLow;
   double tp = ask + (atr_value*atr_multi_tp5);
      
      

   int candle_condition = 0;
   double open2 = iOpen(symbol,indicator5_timeframe_1D,1);
   if(open2 > open){
      candle_condition = 1;
   }
   if(open2 < open){
      candle_condition = -1;
   }  
   
   int candle_condition_L = 0;
   if(high<close && open2 > open){
      candle_condition_L = 1;
   }
   int candle_condition_S = 0;
   if(low>close && open2 < open){
      candle_condition_S = 1;
   }  
   
   if (handle_macd5[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      ResetLastError();
      handle_macd5[SymbolLoop] = iMACD(SymbolArray5[SymbolLoop], indicator5_timeframe_1D, fast_macd_period5, slow_macd_period5, macd_signal_period5, macd_PRICE5);
      if (handle_macd5[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         int err = GetLastError();
         string msg = "Failed to create RSI handle for " + symbol + " (error: " + IntegerToString(err) + ")";
         if (err == 4302)
            msg += " - Symbol needs to be added to Market Watch.";
         Print(msg);
         return;
      }
   }
         // --- Create handle only if needed ---
   if (handle_stoch5[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      ResetLastError();
      handle_stoch5[SymbolLoop] = iStochastic(SymbolArray5[SymbolLoop], indicator5_timeframe_1D, Stochastic_k_period5, Stochastic_D_period5, Stochastic_slowing5, MODE_SMA, Stochastic_PRICE5);
      if (handle_stoch5[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         int err = GetLastError();
         string msg = "Failed to create RSI handle for " + symbol + " (error: " + IntegerToString(err) + ")";
         if (err == 4302)
            msg += " - Symbol needs to be added to Market Watch.";
         Print(msg);
         return;
      }
   }
   
   
   double kValues[]; // Array for %K line
   double dValues[]; // Array for %D line
   int barsToGet = 10; // Number of values to retrieve
   int barIndex = 0;  // For the current bar
   
   // Retrieve the %K value from Buffer 0
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_stoch5[SymbolLoop], 0, barIndex, barsToGet, kValues) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve %K value: ", GetLastError());
   } 
   
   // Retrieve the %D value from Buffer 1
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_stoch5[SymbolLoop], 1, barIndex, barsToGet, dValues) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve %D value: ", GetLastError());
   } 
   bool isKBelow20 = false; // Flag to track if %K has been below 20 in the last 10 values

   // Check if %K has been under 20 in the last 10 values
   for (int i = 0; i < barsToGet; i++) {
       if (kValues[i] < 20) {
           isKBelow20 = true;
           break; // Exit the loop as we only need one instance
       }
   }

   if (handle_rsi5[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      ResetLastError();
      handle_rsi5[SymbolLoop] = iRSI(SymbolArray5[SymbolLoop], indicator5_timeframe_1D, RSIPeriod5, RSI_price5);
      if (handle_rsi5[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         int err = GetLastError();
         string msg = "Failed to create RSI handle for " + symbol + " (error: " + IntegerToString(err) + ")";
         if (err == 4302)
            msg += " - Symbol needs to be added to Market Watch.";
         Print(msg);
         return;
      }
   }

               
   double rsiValue[]; // Adjust size based on the range you need
   int barsToGet1 = 14; // Number of RSI values to retrieve
   int barIndex1 = 0; // Starting from the most recent bar
   
   // Retrieve RSI values
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_rsi5[SymbolLoop], 0, barIndex1, barsToGet1, rsiValue) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve RSI values: ", GetLastError());
       return;
   }
   //int count = ArraySize(rsiValue);
   double averageRSI = CalculateAverage(rsiValue);
   //Print("Average RSI Value: ", averageRSI);
   
   
   double macdLine[];    // Array for MACD line values
   double signalLine[];  // Array for Signal line values
   double histogram[];   // Array for Histogram values
   
   // Retrieve the MACD line value from Buffer 0
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_macd5[SymbolLoop], 0, 0, 3, macdLine) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve MACD line value: ", GetLastError());
   }
   
   // Retrieve the Signal line value from Buffer 1
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_macd5[SymbolLoop], 1, 0, 3, signalLine) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve Signal line value: ", GetLastError());
   } 

   bool macd_crossover = false;
   if(signalLine[0]>signalLine[1] && macdLine[0]<signalLine[1] && macdLine[1]>signalLine[2]){
      macd_crossover = true;
   }
   
   bool macd_crossunder = false;
   if(signalLine[0]<signalLine[1] && macdLine[0]>signalLine[1] && macdLine[1]<signalLine[2]){
      macd_crossunder = true;
   } 
 
 
      
   double sl_thresh = atr_value;
   double profit_thresh = atr_value;
      
   string side = "long"; 
   double TP = tp; 
   double SL = sl;  
   double TrailTP = 0; 
   double TrailThresh = 0;  
   string ExpiryDate = globalTime;
   double nums[20];
   for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
       nums[i] = 0;  
   }
   if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh5 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && rsiValue[0] > averageRSI && macd_crossover && isKBelow20 && kValues[0]>20 && kValues[0]<80 && ask >= (sl+sl_thresh) && tp >= (ask+profit_thresh) ){
      uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray5);
      if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades5){
         trade_entry(comment5_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat5OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L5, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
         arrays5[SymbolLoop][0] = 1 ;
      }
   
   }

    if(position.PositionID!=0){
      if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID))  // Select the position by ticket
      {
         datetime open_time = (datetime)PositionGetInteger(POSITION_TIME);
         
         int elapsedTime = (int)(globalTime - open_time);  // Calculate elapsed time in seconds
         int remainingTime = countdownDuration5 - elapsedTime;          // Calculate remaining time
      
         if(position.PositionID!=0 && remainingTime<=0  ){
            Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
            CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
         }
         
      }
   }
   
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid>position.TP ){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && ask<position.SL ){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }     
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }      
   
   if(!backtest_active){
   LogErrorToCSV();
   }           
}






void stocks_macd_ema_stoch(int SymbolLoop){
   ResetLastError();
   string symbol = SymbolArray4[SymbolLoop];
   int strat_num = 4;
   if(!IsMarketOpen(symbol)){return;};
   int uniqueOriginalIDCount = 0 ;
    
   bool selected = SymbolSelect(symbol, true);
   if(!selected){Print("symbol not in market watch? ", symbol); return;};

   double openPrices[];
   int totalOpenPrices = CopyOpen(symbol, PERIOD_D1, 0, 50, openPrices);
   
   if (totalOpenPrices < 50)
   {
       PrintFormat("Insufficient historical open prices: Only %d available for %s on timeframe %s.",
                   totalOpenPrices, symbol, EnumToString(PERIOD_D1));
       return;
   }

   double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol,SYMBOL_BID);
   double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol,SYMBOL_ASK);
   double spreadPercent = ((ask-bid) / ask) * 100.0;
   double open = iOpen(symbol,indicator4_timeframe_1D,0);
   double close = iClose(symbol,indicator4_timeframe_1D,1);
   double high = iHigh(symbol,indicator4_timeframe_1D,2);
   double low = iLow(symbol,indicator4_timeframe_1D,2);
   
    update_open_symbol4(SymbolLoop);
    if (open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][1] != 1)
    {
        //Print(symbol," symbol is not trading righ now ");
        return;
    }
    

   if (handle_stoch4[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      ResetLastError();
      handle_stoch4[SymbolLoop] = iStochastic(SymbolArray4[SymbolLoop], indicator4_timeframe_1D, Stochastic_k_period4, Stochastic_D_period4, Stochastic_slowing4, MODE_SMA, Stochastic_PRICE4);
      if (handle_stoch4[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         int err = GetLastError();
         string msg = "Failed to create RSI handle for " + symbol + " (error: " + IntegerToString(err) + ")";
         if (err == 4302)
            msg += " - Symbol needs to be added to Market Watch.";
         Print(msg);
         return;
      }
   }
   

   double kValues[]; // Array for %K line
   double dValues[]; // Array for %D line
   int barsToGet = 10; // Number of values to retrieve
   int barIndex = 0;  // For the current bar
   
   // Retrieve the %K value from Buffer 0
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_stoch4[SymbolLoop], 0, barIndex, barsToGet, kValues) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve %K value: ", GetLastError());
   } 
   
   // Retrieve the %D value from Buffer 1
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_stoch4[SymbolLoop], 1, barIndex, barsToGet, dValues) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve %D value: ", GetLastError());
   } 
   bool isKBelow20 = false; // Flag to track if %K has been below 20 in the last 10 values

   // Check if %K has been under 20 in the last 10 values
   for (int i = 0; i < barsToGet; i++) {
       if (kValues[i] < 20) {
           isKBelow20 = true;
           break; // Exit the loop as we only need one instance
       }
   }

   if (handle_EMA4[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      ResetLastError();
      handle_EMA4[SymbolLoop] = iMA(SymbolArray4[SymbolLoop], indicator4_timeframe_1D, EMA_PERIOD4, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_OPEN);
      if (handle_EMA4[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         int err = GetLastError();
         string msg = "Failed to create RSI handle for " + symbol + " (error: " + IntegerToString(err) + ")";
         if (err == 4302)
            msg += " - Symbol needs to be added to Market Watch.";
         Print(msg);
         return;
      }
   }
               
   double emaValue[]; // Array to hold the EMA value
   // Retrieve the EMA value for the current bar
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_EMA4[SymbolLoop], 0, 0, 1, emaValue) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve EMA value: ", GetLastError());
   }

   if (handle_macd4[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      ResetLastError();
      handle_macd4[SymbolLoop] = iMACD(SymbolArray4[SymbolLoop], indicator4_timeframe_1D, fast_macd_period4, slow_macd_period4, macd_signal_period4, macd_PRICE4);
      if (handle_macd4[SymbolLoop] == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         int err = GetLastError();
         string msg = "Failed to create RSI handle for " + symbol + " (error: " + IntegerToString(err) + ")";
         if (err == 4302)
            msg += " - Symbol needs to be added to Market Watch.";
         Print(msg);
         return;
      }
   }
   
   double macdLine[];    // Array for MACD line values
   double signalLine[];  // Array for Signal line values
   
   // Retrieve the MACD line value from Buffer 0
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_macd4[SymbolLoop], 0, 0, 3, macdLine) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve MACD line value: ", GetLastError());
   }
   
   // Retrieve the Signal line value from Buffer 1
   if (CopyBuffer(handle_macd4[SymbolLoop], 1, 0, 3, signalLine) <= 0) {
       Print("Failed to retrieve Signal line value: ", GetLastError());
   }
   

   bool macd_crossover = false;
   if(signalLine[0]>signalLine[1] && macdLine[0]<signalLine[1] && macdLine[1]>signalLine[2]){
      macd_crossover = true;
   }
   
   bool macd_crossunder = false;
   if(signalLine[0]<signalLine[1] && macdLine[0]>signalLine[1] && macdLine[1]<signalLine[2]){
      macd_crossunder = true;
   } 
 
   bool ema_down_active = true;
   if(open <= emaValue[0] && EMA_down_FILTER4){
      ema_down_active = false;
   }
   if(open >= emaValue[0] && !EMA_down_FILTER4){
      ema_down_active = false;
   }                
 
   double higharray[], lowarray[], closearray[];
   int count = ATRinput4 + 1;
   if (CopyHigh(symbol, ATRPeriod4, 0, count, higharray) != count ||
       CopyLow(symbol, ATRPeriod4, 0, count, lowarray) != count ||
       CopyClose(symbol, ATRPeriod4, 0, count, closearray) != count)
   {
      Print("Failed to load price data.");
      return;
   }

   ArraySetAsSeries(higharray, true);
   ArraySetAsSeries(lowarray, true);
   ArraySetAsSeries(closearray, true);

   // --- Calculate custom ATR for current bar only ---
   double atr_value = GetCustomATR(higharray, lowarray, closearray, ATRinput4);
   
    ulong positionTicket = 0 ;
    string string_STRAT_NUM = "4";
    string tableName = "Long" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
    int ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
    PositionData position;
    ResetPositionData(position);
    if(arrays4[SymbolLoop][0] != -1){
    
    if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
       else{return;};
      if (position.PositionID != 0)
      {
         arrays4[SymbolLoop][0] = 1 ;
         if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID)) 
         {
            //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
         }
         else
         {
            if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
            int arraydelete[1];
            arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
            Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
            DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
            ResetPositionData(position);
            }
         }
      }
      else
      {
         arrays4[SymbolLoop][0] = -1 ;
      }
   }

   string side = "long"; 
   double TP = 0; 
   double SL = ask - (atr_value*sl_atr_multi4);  
   double TrailTP = 0; 
   double TrailThresh = 0;  
   string ExpiryDate = globalTime;
   double nums[20];
   for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
       nums[i] = 0;  
   }
   if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh4 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && macd_crossover && macdLine[0]<=0 && kValues[0]<=35 && ema_down_active){
      uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray4);
      if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades4){
         trade_entry(comment4_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat4OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L4, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
         arrays4[SymbolLoop][0] = 1 ;
      }
   }
   
    if(position.PositionID!=0){
      if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID))  // Select the position by ticket
      {
         datetime open_time = (datetime)PositionGetInteger(POSITION_TIME);
         
         int elapsedTime = (int)(globalTime - open_time);  // Calculate elapsed time in seconds
         int remainingTime = countdownDuration4 - elapsedTime;          // Calculate remaining time
      
         if(position.PositionID!=0 && remainingTime<=0  ){
            Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
            CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
         }
         
      }
   }
         
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && macd_crossunder){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }     
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && kValues[0]>=65){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }        
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && macdLine[0]>=0){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }       
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid <= position.SL){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }          
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }      
   
   if(!backtest_active){
   LogErrorToCSV();   
   }
            
}

void STOCKS_ROC_ATR(int SymbolLoop){
    string symbol = SymbolArray3[SymbolLoop];
    ResetLastError();
    int uniqueOriginalIDCount = 0 ;

   double openPrices[];
   int totalOpenPrices = CopyOpen(symbol, PERIOD_D1, 0, 50, openPrices);
   
   if (totalOpenPrices < 50)
   {
       PrintFormat("Insufficient historical open prices: Only %d available for %s on timeframe %s.",
                   totalOpenPrices, symbol, EnumToString(PERIOD_D1));
       return;
   }
   int strat_num = 3 ;
   
   if(!IsMarketOpen(symbol)){return;};
   
      bool selected = SymbolSelect(symbol, true);
   if(!selected){Print("symbol not in market watch? ", symbol); return;};

    update_open_symbol3(SymbolLoop);
    if (open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][1] != 1)
    {
        return;
    }
    
    ulong positionTicket = 0 ;
    string string_STRAT_NUM = "3";
    string tableName = "Long" +symbol+string_STRAT_NUM;     // Example table name
    int ordernum = 1; // Example OrderNum to search for    
    PositionData position;
    ResetPositionData(position);
    if(arrays3[SymbolLoop][0] != -1){
    
    if(GetPositionData(dbFile, tableName, position, ordernum, -1)){}
       else{return;};
      if (position.PositionID != 0)
      {
         arrays3[SymbolLoop][0] = 1 ;
         if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID)) 
         {
            //Print("Position is still active. PositionID: ", position.PositionID);
         }
         else
         {
            if(DontResetWhenManualCose){
            int arraydelete[1];
            arraydelete[0] = position.PositionID;
            Print("Position is not active or has expired. Resetting...");
            DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, arraydelete);
            ResetPositionData(position);
            }
         }
      }
      else
      {
         arrays3[SymbolLoop][0] = -1 ;
      }
   }
   
   double high0 = iHigh(symbol,indicator3_timeframe_1D,0);
   double high = iHigh(symbol,indicator3_timeframe_1D,1);
   double close0 = iClose(symbol,indicator3_timeframe_1D,1);
   double open0 = iOpen(symbol,indicator3_timeframe_1D,1);
   double close1 = iClose(symbol,indicator3_timeframe_1D,2);
   double open1 = iOpen(symbol,indicator3_timeframe_1D,2);
   
   bool shortENGULFING_last_candle = false;
   if(close1>open1 && close0<open0 && open0>close1 && close0<open1){
      shortENGULFING_last_candle = true;
   }
   bool longENGULFING_last_candle = false;
   if(close1<open1 && close0>open0 && open0<close1 && close0>open1){
      longENGULFING_last_candle = true;
   }
   bool long_entry_signal = false;
   if(longENGULFING_last_candle || shortENGULFING_last_candle){
      long_entry_signal = true;
   }

   double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol,SYMBOL_BID);
   double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol,SYMBOL_ASK);
   double spreadPercent = ((ask-bid) / ask) * 100.0;
   
   double higharray[], lowarray[], closearray[];
   int count = ATRinput3 + 1;
   if (CopyHigh(symbol, ATRPeriod3, 0, count, higharray) != count ||
       CopyLow(symbol, ATRPeriod3, 0, count, lowarray) != count ||
       CopyClose(symbol, ATRPeriod3, 0, count, closearray) != count)
   {
      Print("Failed to load price data.");
      return;
   }

   ArraySetAsSeries(higharray, true);
   ArraySetAsSeries(lowarray, true);
   ArraySetAsSeries(closearray, true);

   // --- Calculate custom ATR for current bar only ---
   double atr_value = GetCustomATR(higharray, lowarray, closearray, ATRinput3);

   double close[];
   int count2 = ROCPeriod3 + 10;  // Ensure enough candles
   CopyClose(symbol, indicator3_timeframe_1D, 0, count2, close);

   
   ArraySetAsSeries(close, true);
   
   // --- Declare ROC array and initialize size ---
   double roc_values[];
   int rocCount = count2 - ROCPeriod3;
   ArrayResize(roc_values, rocCount);
   
   // --- Calculate and store ROC values ---
   for (int i = 0; i < rocCount; i++)
   {
      roc_values[i] = GetCustomROC(close, ROCPeriod3, i);
      // Optional: Print values
      //Print("ROC[", i, "] = ", roc_values[i]);
   }

   string side = "long"; 
   double TP = ask + ( atr_value*tp_atr_multi); 
   double SL = ask - (atr_value*sl_atr_multi);  
   double TrailTP = 0; 
   double TrailThresh = 0;  
   string ExpiryDate = globalTime;
   double nums[20];
   for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
       nums[i] = 0;  
   }
   if(spreadPercent < spreadPercent_thresh3 && isAutoTradingEnabled && !equityDDlow && !equityDD_hit_close && IsMarketOpen(symbol) && position.PositionID==0 && roc_values[0] <= rocthresh_negative && roc_values[0]>roc_values[1]){
      uniqueOriginalIDCount = CountUniqueOriginalIDs(dbFile, strat_num, SymbolArray3);
      if(uniqueOriginalIDCount < max_trades3){
         trade_entry(comment3_input, tableName, symbol, side, strat_num, ordernum, ask, bid, strat3OrderSizeMultiplyer, InpLots_L3, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, ExpiryDate, nums);
         arrays3[SymbolLoop][0] = 1 ;
      }
   }

   if(position.PositionID!=0){
      if (PositionSelectByTicket(position.PositionID))  // Select the position by ticket
      {
         datetime open_time = (datetime)PositionGetInteger(POSITION_TIME);
         
         int elapsedTime = (int)(globalTime - open_time);  // Calculate elapsed time in seconds
         int remainingTime = countdownDuration3 - elapsedTime;          // Calculate remaining time
      
         if(position.PositionID!=0 && remainingTime<=0  ){
            Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
            CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
         }
      }
   }
   

   if(position.PositionID!=0 && ask < position.SL ){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && bid > position.TP ){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }
   if(position.PositionID!=0 && equityDD_hit_close){
      Print("closing symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 );
      CloseAllOrders2(tableName , position.PositionID);
   }   
   if(!backtest_active){
   LogErrorToCSV();
   }
   
}

double CalculateATR(string symbol, ENUM_TIMEFRAMES timeframe, int atr_period)
{
   double atr_sum = 0;
   for(int i = 0; i < atr_period; i++)
   {
      double high = iHigh(symbol, timeframe, i);
      double low  = iLow(symbol, timeframe, i);
      double close_prev = iClose(symbol, timeframe, i+1);

      double tr = MathMax(high - low, 
                  MathMax(MathAbs(high - close_prev), 
                          MathAbs(low - close_prev)));

      atr_sum += tr;
   }
   return atr_sum / atr_period;  // Simple Moving Average of TR
}

void DeleteOldDatabase(string dbFile)
{
    if (FileIsExist(dbFile, FILE_COMMON))  // Check if the file exists in the Common folder
    {
        if (FileDelete(dbFile))
            Print("Database deleted successfully: ", dbFile);
        else
            Print("Failed to delete database. Error: ", GetLastError());
    }
}

void RecordSentimentToDB(string dbFile, double Total_Per, double s_N, double s_NEU, double s_P, 
                         double R_s_N, double R_s_NEU, double R_s_P, 
                         string SymbolLoop, double OpenPrice)
{
    // Open or create the SQLite database
    int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE | DATABASE_OPEN_CREATE);
    if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
    {
        Print("Failed to open database: ", dbFile, ". Error: ", GetLastError());
        return;
    }

    // Ensure the table exists
    string createTableQuery =
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS SentimentData ("
        "ID INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "
        "Timestamp INTEGER NOT NULL, "  // Store as UNIX timestamp
        "Total_Per REAL NOT NULL, "
        "s_N REAL NOT NULL, "
        "s_NEU REAL NOT NULL, "
        "s_P REAL NOT NULL, "
        "R_s_N REAL NOT NULL, "
        "R_s_NEU REAL NOT NULL, "
        "R_s_P REAL NOT NULL, "
        "Symbol TEXT NOT NULL, "
        "OpenPrice REAL NOT NULL)";  // New column for Open Price

    if (!DatabaseExecute(db, createTableQuery))
    {
        Print("Failed to create table. Error: ", GetLastError());
        DatabaseClose(db);
        return;
    }

    // Get current timestamp
    datetime now = TimeCurrent();

    // Insert sentiment record
    string insertQuery = "INSERT INTO SentimentData (Timestamp, Total_Per, s_N, s_NEU, s_P, "
                         "R_s_N, R_s_NEU, R_s_P, Symbol, OpenPrice) VALUES (" +
                         IntegerToString(now) + ", " +
                         DoubleToString(Total_Per, 4) + ", " +
                         DoubleToString(s_N, 4) + ", " +
                         DoubleToString(s_NEU, 4) + ", " +
                         DoubleToString(s_P, 4) + ", " +
                         DoubleToString(R_s_N, 4) + ", " +
                         DoubleToString(R_s_NEU, 4) + ", " +
                         DoubleToString(R_s_P, 4) + ", '" +
                         SymbolLoop + "', " +
                         DoubleToString(OpenPrice, 5) + ")";  // Add OpenPrice

    if (!DatabaseExecute(db, insertQuery))
    {
        Print("Failed to insert sentiment data. Error: ", GetLastError());
    }

    // Close the database
    DatabaseClose(db);
}








//##################################################################################################################################################################
//##################################################################################################################################################################


double CalculateRisk(string symbol, string side, double entryPrice, double stopLossPrice, double lotSize)
{
   // SL must be set
   if(stopLossPrice == 0)
   {
      Print("Error: SL is zero – cannot calculate risk.");
      return -1;
   }

   // Get contract size
   double contractSize = 0.0;
   if(!SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_TRADE_CONTRACT_SIZE, contractSize))
   {
      Print("Error: Unable to retrieve contract size for ", symbol);
      return -1;
   }

   // Price difference
   double priceDiff = 0.0;
   if(side == "long")
      priceDiff = entryPrice - stopLossPrice;
   else if(side == "short")
      priceDiff = stopLossPrice - entryPrice;
   else
   {
      Print("Error: Invalid trade side: ", side);
      return -1;
   }

   // Risk must be positive
   if(priceDiff <= 0)
   {
      Print("Error: Invalid SL for ", side, " – price difference is non-positive.");
      return -1;
   }

   // Calculate monetary risk
   double risk = priceDiff * lotSize * contractSize;
   return risk;
}

void trade_entry(string comment, string tableName, string symbol, string side, int strat_num, int ordernum, double ask, double bid, 
                 double stratOrderSizeMultiplyer, double InpLots, double TP, double SL, double TrailTP, double TrailThresh, 
                 string ExpiryDate, double &nums[]) {   
     ulong positionTicket = 0;
     if (side == "long"){
     
      Print("opening symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num, " spread ", CalculatePercentageSpread(bid, ask) );
      double lots, Remaininglots;
      if(!CalculateLots_L(ask, symbol, lots, Remaininglots, (InpLots*baseOrderSizeMultiplyer)*stratOrderSizeMultiplyer )){return;}
       if (CanPlaceOrder(symbol, lots))
       {
       }
       else
       {
           Print("Cannot place order for ", symbol);
           return;
       }
      double margin;
      double riskAmount = CalculateRisk(symbol, side, ask, SL, lots);
      if(riskAmount == -1){Print("ERROR risk calculation");return;}
      
      if(OrderCalcMargin(ORDER_TYPE_BUY, symbol,lots,ask,margin) && margin + riskAmount > AccountInfoDouble(ACCOUNT_MARGIN_FREE)*1.001){
         Print("ERROR not enough margin !");
         return;
      }
      if(trade.Buy(lots,symbol,ask, 0 , 0 ,comment)){
         positionTicket = trade.ResultOrder(); // Get the ticket for the opened order
         PositionData position;
         position.Table = tableName;
         position.PositionID = positionTicket;
         position.TP = TP;
         position.SL = SL;
         position.TrailTP = TrailTP;
         position.TrailThresh = TrailThresh;
         position.Lots = lots;
         position.OrderTime = globalTime;
         position.Side = "long";
         position.OriginalID = positionTicket;
         position.symbol = symbol;
         position.OrderNum = ordernum;
         position.StratNum = strat_num;
         position.Price = ask;
         position.ExpiryDate = ExpiryDate;
      
        for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
            position.Nums[i] = nums[i];  // Copy input array into struct
        }
      
         // Call the function to insert the row into the table
         Insertdata(position, dbFile, symbol, strat_num);
         
         Print("trade opened symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 , " spread ", CalculatePercentageSpread(bid, ask));
      }

      // Loop to place multiple trades if there are remaining lots
      while (Remaininglots > 0)
      {
          double max = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_VOLUME_MAX);
          double currentLots = MathMin(max, Remaininglots); // Use the smaller of `lots` or `remainingLots`
      
          // Check margin availability
          double margin;
          double riskAmount = CalculateRisk(symbol, side, ask, SL, lots);
          if(riskAmount == -1){Print("ERROR risk calculation");return;}
          if (OrderCalcMargin(ORDER_TYPE_BUY, symbol, currentLots, ask, margin) && margin + riskAmount > AccountInfoDouble(ACCOUNT_MARGIN_FREE)*1.001)
          {
              Print("ERROR: Not enough margin for current lot size!");
              break; // Exit the loop if there's insufficient margin
          }
      
          // Place the trade
          if (trade.Buy(currentLots, symbol, ask, 0, 0, comment + "plus"))
          {
              ulong positionTicket2 = trade.ResultOrder(); // Get the ticket for the opened order
      
               PositionData position;
               position.Table = tableName;
               position.PositionID = positionTicket2;
               position.TP = TP;
               position.SL = SL;
               position.TrailTP = TrailTP;
               position.TrailThresh = TrailThresh;
               position.Lots = lots;
               position.OrderTime = globalTime;
               position.Side = "long";
               position.OriginalID = positionTicket;
               position.symbol = symbol;
               position.OrderNum = ordernum;
               position.StratNum = strat_num;
               position.Price = ask;
               position.ExpiryDate = ExpiryDate;
                  
              for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
                  position.Nums[i] = nums[i];  // Copy input array into struct
              }
            
               // Call the function to insert the row into the table
               Insertdata(position, dbFile, symbol, strat_num);
      
              // Update remaining lots
              Remaininglots -= currentLots;
              PrintFormat("Order placed successfully: Symbol=%s, Lots=%.2f, RemainingLots=%.2f", symbol, currentLots, Remaininglots);
          }
          else
          {
              PrintFormat("Failed to place order for %s. Error: %d", symbol, GetLastError());
              break; // Exit the loop if the order fails
          }
      }
      
      if (Remaininglots > 0)
      {
          PrintFormat("Not all remaining lots were placed. RemainingLots=%.2f", Remaininglots);
      }
    }
    else{
       if (side == "short"){
          
          Print("opening symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num, " spread ", CalculatePercentageSpread(bid, ask) );
         double lots, Remaininglots;
         if(!CalculateLots_L(bid, symbol, lots, Remaininglots, (InpLots*baseOrderSizeMultiplyer)*stratOrderSizeMultiplyer)){return;}
          if (CanPlaceOrder(symbol, lots))
          {
          }
          else
          {
              Print("Cannot place order for ", symbol);
              return;
          }
         double margin;
         double riskAmount = CalculateRisk(symbol, side, bid, SL, lots);   
         if(riskAmount == -1){Print("ERROR risk calculation");return;}  
         if(OrderCalcMargin(ORDER_TYPE_SELL, symbol,lots,bid,margin) && margin + riskAmount > AccountInfoDouble(ACCOUNT_MARGIN_FREE)*1.001){
            Print("ERROR not enough margin !");
            return;
         }
         if(trade.Sell(lots,symbol,bid, 0, 0,comment)){
            
            positionTicket = trade.ResultOrder(); // Get the ticket for the opened order
            PositionData position;
            position.Table = tableName;
            position.PositionID = positionTicket;
            position.TP = TP;
            position.SL = SL;
            position.TrailTP = TrailTP;
            position.TrailThresh = TrailThresh;
            position.Lots = lots;
            position.OrderTime = globalTime;
            position.Side = "short";
            position.OriginalID = positionTicket;
            position.symbol = symbol;
            position.OrderNum = ordernum;
            position.StratNum = strat_num;
            position.Price = ask;
            position.ExpiryDate = ExpiryDate;
         
           for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
               position.Nums[i] = nums[i];  // Copy input array into struct
           }
         
            // Call the function to insert the row into the table
            Insertdata(position, dbFile, symbol, strat_num);
            
            Print("trade opened symbol " ,symbol, " strategy ", strat_num , " ID ", position.PositionID, " side ", position.Side, " lots ", position.Lots, " open Price ", position.Price, " current mid Price ", (bid+ask)/2 , " spread ", CalculatePercentageSpread(bid, ask));
         }
      
         // Loop to place multiple trades if there are remaining lots
         while (Remaininglots > 0)
         {
             double max = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_VOLUME_MAX);
             double currentLots = MathMin(max, Remaininglots); // Use the smaller of `lots` or `remainingLots`
         
             // Check margin availability
             double margin;
             double riskAmount = CalculateRisk(symbol, side, bid, SL, lots);
             if(riskAmount == -1){Print("ERROR risk calculation");return;}
             if (OrderCalcMargin(ORDER_TYPE_SELL, symbol, currentLots, bid, margin) && margin + riskAmount > AccountInfoDouble(ACCOUNT_MARGIN_FREE)*1.001)
             {
                 Print("ERROR: Not enough margin for current lot size!");
                 break; // Exit the loop if there's insufficient margin
             }
         
             // Place the trade
             if (trade.Sell(currentLots, symbol, bid, 0, 0, comment + "plus"))
             {
                  ulong positionTicket2 = trade.ResultOrder(); // Get the ticket for the opened order
                  PositionData position;
                  position.Table = tableName;
                  position.PositionID = positionTicket2;
                  position.TP = TP;
                  position.SL = SL;
                  position.TrailTP = TrailTP;
                  position.TrailThresh = TrailThresh;
                  position.Lots = lots;
                  position.OrderTime = globalTime;
                  position.Side = "short";
                  position.OriginalID = positionTicket;
                  position.symbol = symbol;
                  position.OrderNum = ordernum;
                  position.StratNum = strat_num;
                  position.Price = ask;
                  position.ExpiryDate = ExpiryDate;
                 for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
                     position.Nums[i] = nums[i];  // Copy input array into struct
                 }
               
                  // Call the function to insert the row into the table
                  Insertdata(position, dbFile, symbol, strat_num);
                 // Update remaining lots
                 Remaininglots -= currentLots;
                 PrintFormat("Order placed successfully: Symbol=%s, Lots=%.2f, RemainingLots=%.2f", symbol, currentLots, Remaininglots);
             }
             else
             {
                 PrintFormat("Failed to place order for %s. Error: %d", symbol, GetLastError());
                 break; // Exit the loop if the order fails
             }
         }
         
         if (Remaininglots > 0)
         {
             PrintFormat("Not all remaining lots were placed. RemainingLots=%.2f", Remaininglots);
         }
         
       }

       else{
         PrintFormat("trade open error side not met", side);
       }
  
   }
}
