bool FolderExists(string folder)
{
   ResetLastError();
   int handle = FileFindFirst("*.*", folder);
   bool exists = (handle != INVALID_HANDLE);
   FileFindClose(handle);
   return exists;
}


void DeleteDatabaseFile(string dbFile)
{
   // Check if the file exists
   if (FileIsExist(dbFile))
   {
      // Attempt to delete the file
      if (FileDelete(dbFile))
      {
         Print("File deleted successfully: ", dbFile);
      }
      else
      {
         Print("Failed to delete file: ", dbFile, ". Error: ", GetLastError());
      }
   }
   else
   {
      Print("File does not exist: ", dbFile);
   }
}




void ResetPositionData(PositionData &position)
{
   position.Table = "";
   position.PositionID = 0;
   position.TP = 0.0;
   position.SL = 0.0;
   position.TrailTP = 0.0;
   position.TrailThresh = 0.0;
   position.Lots = 0.0;
   position.OrderTime = 0; // Default datetime value
   position.Side = "";     // Default string value
   position.OriginalID = 0;
   position.symbol = "";   // Default string value
   position.OrderNum = 0;
   position.StratNum = 0;
   position.Price = 0.0;
   position.ExpiryDate = 0; // Default datetime value

   // Reset Num1 to Num20 to 0.0
   for(int i = 0; i < 20; i++)
   {
      position.Nums[i] = 0.0;
   }
}


//  done
void CreatePositionTables(string dbFile)
{
   int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE | DATABASE_OPEN_CREATE);
   if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to open database: ", dbFile, ". Error: ", GetLastError());
      return; // Exit if the database cannot be opened
   }
   if (!CreateTable(db, table_default))
      Print("Error creating table: ", table_default);

   DatabaseClose(db); // Simply call DatabaseClose
}

//  done
bool CreateTable(int db, string tableName)
{
   // SQL query to create a table
   string createTableQuery =
      "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS " + tableName + " ("
      "TableName TEXT NOT NULL, " 
      "PositionID INTEGER NOT NULL, " 
      "TP REAL NOT NULL, "
      "SL REAL NOT NULL, "
      "TrailTP REAL NOT NULL, "
      "TrailThresh REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Lots REAL NOT NULL, "
      "OrderTime TEXT NOT NULL, "
      "Side TEXT NOT NULL, "
      "OriginalID INTEGER NOT NULL, "
      "Symbol TEXT NOT NULL, "
      "OrderNum INTEGER NOT NULL, "
      "StratNum INTEGER NOT NULL, "
      "Price REAL NOT NULL, "
      "ExpiryDate TEXT NOT NULL, "
      "Num1 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num2 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num3 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num4 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num5 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num6 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num7 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num8 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num9 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num10 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num11 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num12 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num13 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num14 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num15 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num16 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num17 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num18 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num19 REAL NOT NULL, "
      "Num20 REAL NOT NULL"
      ")";

   // Execute the query and return success or failure
   if (!DatabaseExecute(db, createTableQuery))
   {
      Print("Failed to create table: ", tableName, ". SQL: ", createTableQuery, ". Error: ", GetLastError());
      return false;
   }

   return true;
}

void GetTableNames(string dbFile, string &tableNames[]) 
{
   // Open the SQLite database
   int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE);
   if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to open database: ", GetLastError());
      return;
   }

   // Query to get all table names
   string query = "SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table';";

   // Prepare the query
   int stmt = DatabasePrepare(db, query);
   if (stmt == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to prepare query: ", GetLastError());
      DatabaseClose(db);
      return;
   }

   // Clear the output array before storing table names
   ArrayResize(tableNames, 0);

   // Read and store table names
   while (DatabaseRead(stmt))  // Reads one row at a time
   {
      string tableName = "";  // Declare a string variable

      if (DatabaseColumnText(stmt, 0, tableName))  // Pass it by reference
      {
         // Resize the array to add a new table name
         int newSize = ArraySize(tableNames) + 1;
         ArrayResize(tableNames, newSize);
         
         // Store the table name in the array
         tableNames[newSize - 1] = tableName;
      }
   }

   // Close the statement and database
   DatabaseFinalize(stmt);
   DatabaseClose(db);
}




int CountUniqueOriginalIDs(string dbFile, int strat_num, string &symbols[])
{

   int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE);
   if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to open database: ", GetLastError());
      return 0;
   }

   ulong uniqueOriginalIDs[];  // Array to store unique OriginalIDs

   // Loop through each symbol and check both Long and Short tables
   for (int i = 0; i < ArraySize(symbols); i++)
   {
      string longTable = "Long" + symbols[i] + IntegerToString(strat_num);
      string shortTable = "Short" + symbols[i] + IntegerToString(strat_num);
      
      // Collect OriginalIDs from both tables
      GetOriginalIDsFromTable(db, longTable, uniqueOriginalIDs);
      GetOriginalIDsFromTable(db, shortTable, uniqueOriginalIDs);
   }

   // Get the total count of unique OriginalIDs
   int uniqueCount = ArraySize(uniqueOriginalIDs);

   // Close the database
   DatabaseClose(db);

   //Print("Total unique OriginalIDs for strat_num ", strat_num, ": ", uniqueCount);
   return uniqueCount;
}




// done
bool GetOriginalIDsFromTable(int db, string Table, ulong &originalIDs[])
{
   // Format query manually instead of using parameter binding
   string query = "SELECT DISTINCT OriginalID FROM '" + table_default + "' WHERE TableName = '" + Table + "'";

   int statement = DatabasePrepare(db, query);
   if (statement == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to prepare query for table: ", Table);
      return false;
   }

   while (DatabaseRead(statement))
   {
      int tempID = 0;  // SQLite stores integers as signed int

      if (DatabaseColumnInteger(statement, 0, tempID))  // Get OriginalID
      {
         ulong originalID = (ulong)tempID;  // Convert to ulong safely

         // Check if the ID is already in the array (avoid duplicates)
         if (!ArrayContains(originalIDs, originalID))
         {
            int size = ArraySize(originalIDs);
            ArrayResize(originalIDs, size + 1);
            originalIDs[size] = originalID;
         }
      }
   }

   DatabaseFinalize(statement);
   return true;
}


// Helper function to check if value exists in array
bool ArrayContains(const ulong &arr[], ulong value)
{
   for (int i = 0; i < ArraySize(arr); i++)
   {
      if (arr[i] == value)
         return true;
   }
   return false;
}




void GetAllPositionIDs(string dbFile, ulong &positionIDs[])
{
   // Open the SQLite database
   int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE);
   if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to open database: ", GetLastError());
      return;
   }

   // Clear the output array before storing data
   ArrayResize(positionIDs, 0);

   // Query to select all PositionID values from the table
   string query = "SELECT PositionID FROM " + table_default + ";";

   // Prepare the SQL query
   int stmt = DatabasePrepare(db, query);
   if (stmt == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to prepare query. Error: ", GetLastError());
      DatabaseClose(db);
      return;
   }

   // Read and store PositionID values
   while (DatabaseRead(stmt))
   {
      long posID = 0;

      // Fetch PositionID as long to ensure full range
      if (DatabaseColumnLong(stmt, 0, posID))
      {
         int newSize = ArraySize(positionIDs) + 1;
         ArrayResize(positionIDs, newSize);
         positionIDs[newSize - 1] = (ulong)posID;
      }
   }

   // Finalize the statement and close the database
   DatabaseFinalize(stmt);
   DatabaseClose(db);
}



// done
void DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(string dbFile, int &positionIDs[])
{
   // Open the SQLite database
   int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE);
   if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to open database: ", GetLastError());
      return;
   }

   // If the array is empty, no need to proceed
   int idCount = ArraySize(positionIDs);
   if (idCount == 0)
   {
      Print("No PositionIDs provided for deletion.");
      DatabaseClose(db);
      return;
   }

   // Construct a bulk DELETE query using IN (...)
   string deleteQuery = "DELETE FROM " + table_default + " WHERE PositionID IN (";

   for (int i = 0; i < idCount; i++)
   {
      deleteQuery += IntegerToString(positionIDs[i]);
      if (i < idCount - 1) deleteQuery += ", ";  // Add comma between IDs
   }
   deleteQuery += ")"; // Close the IN clause

   // Execute the delete query
   if (DatabaseExecute(db, deleteQuery))
   {
      //Print("Deleted rows successfully");
   }
   else
   {
      Print("Failed to delete rows from table: ", table_default, ". Error: ", GetLastError());
   }

   // Close the database connection
   DatabaseClose(db);
}



//  done
void FindPositionIDsByOriginalID(string dbFile, int originalID, int &positionIDs[])
{
   // Open the SQLite database
   int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE);
   if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to open database: ", GetLastError());
      return;
   }

   // SQL query to find PositionIDs for the given OriginalID
   string query = "SELECT PositionID FROM " + table_default + " WHERE OriginalID = " + IntegerToString(originalID);

   // Prepare the query
   int statement = DatabasePrepare(db, query);
   if (statement == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to prepare query: ", GetLastError());
      DatabaseClose(db);
      return;
   }

   // Temporary array for PositionIDs
   int tempArray[];
   int positionID;

   // Execute the query and read the results
   while (DatabaseRead(statement))
   {
      if (DatabaseColumnInteger(statement, 0, positionID))  // Correctly fetch value into positionID
      {
         // Append positionID to tempArray
         int size = ArraySize(tempArray);
         ArrayResize(tempArray, size + 1);
         tempArray[size] = positionID;
      }
   }

   // Finalize the statement
   DatabaseFinalize(statement);
   DatabaseClose(db);

   // Copy tempArray to positionIDs
   ArrayFree(positionIDs);  // Clear the original array
   int finalSize = ArraySize(tempArray);
   ArrayResize(positionIDs, finalSize);
   ArrayCopy(positionIDs, tempArray);

   // Debug output: print the retrieved PositionIDs
   if (finalSize > 0)
   {
      //Print("Found ", finalSize, " PositionIDs for OriginalID=", originalID, ":");
      for (int i = 0; i < finalSize; i++)
      {
         //Print("PositionID[", i, "] = ", positionIDs[i]);
      }
   }
   else
   {
      Print("No PositionIDs found for OriginalID=", originalID);
   }
}

// done
bool Insertdata(PositionData &position, string dbFile, string symbol, int strat_num)
{
   // Step 2: Open or create the database
   int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE | DATABASE_OPEN_CREATE);
   if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to open or create database: ", dbFile, ". Error: ", GetLastError());
   }
   //Print("Database opened successfully: ", dbFile);
   
   //string table = side+symbol+IntegerToString(strat_num);

   //CreatePositionTables(dbFile);
   //Print("Table created successfully. ", table);
   
   
//   string longTableName = "Long" + symbol + IntegerToString(strat_num);
//   string shortTableName = "Short" + symbol + IntegerToString(strat_num);
//   
//   if(position.Side=="long"){
//      table = longTableName;
//   }
//   if(position.Side=="Short"){
//      table = shortTableName;
//   }
      
   // Convert datetime to string format for SQLite
   string orderTimeStr = TimeToString(position.OrderTime, TIME_SECONDS);
   string expiryDateStr = TimeToString(position.ExpiryDate, TIME_SECONDS);

   // Construct the SQL query dynamically
   string insertQuery = "INSERT INTO " +table_default+ " (TableName, PositionID, TP, SL, TrailTP, TrailThresh, Lots, OrderTime, Side, OriginalID, Symbol, OrderNum, StratNum, Price, ExpiryDate, ";
   
   // Add column names for Nums[20]
   for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++)
   {
      insertQuery += "Num" + IntegerToString(i + 1);
      if (i < 19) insertQuery += ", ";
   }
   insertQuery += ") VALUES (";
   
   // Add main values
   insertQuery += StringFormat("'%s',%d, %.5f, %.5f, %.5f, %.5f, %.2f, '%s', '%s', %d, '%s', %d, %d, %.5f, '%s', ",
                   position.Table, position.PositionID, position.TP, position.SL, position.TrailTP, position.TrailThresh, position.Lots, orderTimeStr, position.Side,
                   position.OriginalID, position.symbol, position.OrderNum, position.StratNum, position.Price, expiryDateStr);

   // Add Nums[20] values dynamically
   for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++)
   {
      insertQuery += DoubleToString(position.Nums[i], 5);
      if (i < 19) insertQuery += ", ";
   }
   insertQuery += ");";


   // Step 4: Insert the number 1 into the column "number1"
   //string insertQuery = "INSERT INTO LongETHUSD1 (number1) VALUES (1)";
   if (!DatabaseExecute(db, insertQuery))
   {
      Print("Failed to insert into table Error: ", GetLastError());
      DatabaseClose(db);
      return false;
   }
   //Print("Successfully inserted into database ");

   // Step 5: Close the database
   DatabaseClose(db);
   //Print("Database closed successfully.", table);
   
   // Data successfully retrieved
   return true;
}


// done
bool UpdateData(PositionData &position, string dbFile, string symbol, int strat_num)
{
   // Open the SQLite database
   int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE);
   if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to open database: ", dbFile, ". Error: ", GetLastError());
      return false;
   }
   
   // Convert datetime to string format for SQLite
   string orderTimeStr = TimeToString(position.OrderTime, TIME_SECONDS);
   string expiryDateStr = TimeToString(position.ExpiryDate, TIME_SECONDS);

   // Construct the SQL UPDATE query
   string updateQuery = "UPDATE " + table_default + " SET "
                        "TableName = '" + position.Table + "', "  //
                        "TP = " + DoubleToString(position.TP, 5) + ", "
                        "SL = " + DoubleToString(position.SL, 5) + ", "
                        "TrailTP = " + DoubleToString(position.TrailTP, 5) + ", "
                        "TrailThresh = " + DoubleToString(position.TrailThresh, 5) + ", "
                        "Lots = " + DoubleToString(position.Lots, 2) + ", "
                        "OrderTime = '" + orderTimeStr + "', "
                        "Side = '" + position.Side + "', "
                        "OriginalID = " + IntegerToString(position.OriginalID) + ", "
                        "Symbol = '" + position.symbol + "', "
                        "OrderNum = " + IntegerToString(position.OrderNum) + ", "
                        "StratNum = " + IntegerToString(position.StratNum) + ", "
                        "Price = " + DoubleToString(position.Price, 5) + ", "
                        "ExpiryDate = '" + expiryDateStr + "', ";

   // Add Nums[20] values dynamically
   for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++)
   {
      updateQuery += "Num" + IntegerToString(i + 1) + " = " + DoubleToString(position.Nums[i], 5);
      if (i < 19) updateQuery += ", ";  // Add commas between assignments
   }

   // Add WHERE clause to identify the row to update
   updateQuery += " WHERE PositionID = " + IntegerToString(position.PositionID) + ";";

   // Execute the update query
   if (!DatabaseExecute(db, updateQuery))
   {
      Print("Failed to update row for PositionID=", position.PositionID, " in table ", table_default, ". Error: ", GetLastError());
      DatabaseClose(db);
      return false;
   }

   Print("Successfully updated row for PositionID=", position.PositionID, " in table ", table_default);
   
   // Close the database
   DatabaseClose(db);
   return true;
}



bool GetPositionData(string dbFile, string tableName, PositionData &position, int ordernum = -1, int positionID = -1)
{
   int lastError = GetLastError();
   if (lastError != 0 && lastError != 5126) { LogErrorToCSV(); ResetLastError(); }

   // Ensure at least one of TableName, OriginalID, or PositionID is provided
   if (tableName == "" && ordernum == -1 && positionID == -1)
   {
      Print("Error: Either TableName, OriginalID, or PositionID must be provided.");
      ResetPositionData(position);
      if (GetLastError() == 5126 && ignor5126) { ResetLastError(); }
      return false;
   }

   // Open the SQLite database
   int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE);
   if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to open database: ", GetLastError());
      ResetPositionData(position);
      if (GetLastError() == 5126 && ignor5126) { ResetLastError(); }
      return false;
   }

   // Sanitize table_default name to prevent SQL injection
   StringReplace(table_default, "'", "''");
   
   // Construct SQL query based on provided filters
   string query = "SELECT * FROM " + table_default + " WHERE TableName = '" + tableName + "'";
   
   // Add additional conditions if OrderNum or PositionID is provided
   if (ordernum != -1)
   {
      query += " AND OrderNum = " + IntegerToString(ordernum);
   }
   else if (positionID != -1)  // Ensure correct variable name
   {
      query += " AND PositionID = " + IntegerToString(positionID);
   }
   
   

   // Prepare the SQL query
   int statement = DatabasePrepare(db, query);
   if (statement == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("Failed to prepare query: ", GetLastError());
      DatabaseClose(db);
      ResetPositionData(position);
      if (GetLastError() == 5126 && ignor5126) { ResetLastError(); }
      return false;
   }

   // Execute and read the first row (assuming unique PositionID/OriginalID/TableName)
   if (DatabaseRead(statement))
   {
      // ✅ Retrieve "Table" column (1st column)
      DatabaseColumnText(statement, 0, position.Table);

      // ✅ Read all columns
      DatabaseColumnInteger(statement, 1, position.PositionID);
      DatabaseColumnDouble(statement, 2, position.TP);
      DatabaseColumnDouble(statement, 3, position.SL);
      DatabaseColumnDouble(statement, 4, position.TrailTP);
      DatabaseColumnDouble(statement, 5, position.TrailThresh);
      DatabaseColumnDouble(statement, 6, position.Lots);

      string orderTimeStr, expiryDateStr;
      DatabaseColumnText(statement, 7, orderTimeStr);
      DatabaseColumnText(statement, 14, expiryDateStr);

      position.OrderTime = StringToTime(orderTimeStr);
      DatabaseColumnText(statement, 8, position.Side);
      DatabaseColumnInteger(statement, 9, position.OriginalID);
      DatabaseColumnText(statement, 10, position.symbol);
      DatabaseColumnInteger(statement, 11, position.OrderNum);
      DatabaseColumnInteger(statement, 12, position.StratNum);
      DatabaseColumnDouble(statement, 13, position.Price);
      position.ExpiryDate = StringToTime(expiryDateStr);

      // ✅ Read Nums[20]
      for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++)
      {
         DatabaseColumnDouble(statement, 15 + i, position.Nums[i]);
      }
   }
   else
   {
      ResetPositionData(position);
      //Print("No matching data found in table_default for given parameters.");
   }

   // Finalize and close the database
   DatabaseFinalize(statement);
   DatabaseClose(db);
   if (GetLastError() == 5126 && ignor5126) { ResetLastError(); }
   return true;
}




// Function to add a new value to the array
void AddToArray(int &arr[], int newValue)
{
   int size = ArraySize(arr);         // Get the current size of the array
   ArrayResize(arr, size + 1);        // Increase the array size by 1
   arr[size] = newValue;              // Assign the new value to the last position
}



void GetActivePositionsAndOrders(int magicNumber, ulong &positionIDs[], ulong &orderIDs[])
{
   // Clear output arrays before storing new data
   ArrayResize(positionIDs, 0);
   ArrayResize(orderIDs, 0);

   // --- Retrieve Active Positions ---
   for (int i = 0; i < PositionsTotal(); i++)
   {
      if (PositionSelect(PositionGetSymbol(i)))  // Select position by symbol
      {
         int positionMagic = (int)PositionGetInteger(POSITION_MAGIC);
         if (positionMagic == magicNumber)  // Filter by Magic Number
         {
            ulong positionID = PositionGetInteger(POSITION_TICKET);  // Get Position ID

            // Resize and store Position ID
            int newSize = ArraySize(positionIDs) + 1;
            ArrayResize(positionIDs, newSize);
            positionIDs[newSize - 1] = positionID;
         }
      }
   }

   // --- Retrieve Active Orders ---
   for (int i = 0; i < OrdersTotal(); i++)
   {
      ulong ticket = OrderGetTicket(i);  // Get Order Ticket
      if (OrderSelect(ticket))  // Select order by ticket
      {
         int orderMagic = (int)OrderGetInteger(ORDER_MAGIC);
         if (orderMagic == magicNumber)  // Filter by Magic Number
         {
            ulong orderID = OrderGetInteger(ORDER_TICKET);  // Get Order ID

            // Resize and store Order ID
            int newSize = ArraySize(orderIDs) + 1;
            ArrayResize(orderIDs, newSize);
            orderIDs[newSize - 1] = orderID;
         }
      }
   }
}


void FindMissingTradeIDs(const ulong &positionIDList[], const ulong &positionList[], const ulong &orderList[], ulong &missingIDs[])
{
   // Clear the output array before storing new data
   ArrayResize(missingIDs, 0);

   // --- Check Positions ---
   for (int i = 0; i < ArraySize(positionList); i++)
   {
      if (!IsIDInArray(positionList[i], positionIDList))
      {
         AddToArray2(missingIDs, positionList[i]);
      }
   }

   // --- Check Orders ---
   for (int i = 0; i < ArraySize(orderList); i++)
   {
      if (!IsIDInArray(orderList[i], positionIDList))
      {
         AddToArray2(missingIDs, orderList[i]);
      }
   }
}

// Function to check if an ID exists in an array
bool IsIDInArray(ulong id, const ulong &array[])
{
   for (int i = 0; i < ArraySize(array); i++)
   {
      if (array[i] == id)
         return true;  // Found ID
   }
   return false;  // ID not found
}

// Function to add an ID to an array dynamically
void AddToArray2(ulong &array[], ulong id)
{
   int newSize = ArraySize(array) + 1;
   ArrayResize(array, newSize);
   array[newSize - 1] = id;
}

double CalculatePercentageSpread(double value1, double value2)
{
   if (value1 == 0 && value2 == 0)
      return 0;  // Avoid division by zero

   double spread = fabs(value1 - value2);  // Absolute difference
   double average = (value1 + value2) / 2.0;  // Average of both values

   return (spread / average) * 100.0;  // Percentage Spread
}
    

double GetCustomROC(const double &close[], int period, int shift)
{
   int size = ArraySize(close);
   if (size <= period + shift)
      return EMPTY_VALUE;

   double current = close[shift];
   double past = close[shift + period];

   if (past == 0.0)
      return EMPTY_VALUE;

   return ((current - past) / past) * 100.0;
}


double GetCustomATR(const double &high[], const double &low[], const double &close[], int period)
{
   int size = ArraySize(high);
   if (size < period + 1 || ArraySize(low) != size || ArraySize(close) != size)
      return EMPTY_VALUE;

   double atr = 0.0;
   for (int i = period - 1; i >= 0; i--)
   {
      double highLow   = high[i] - low[i];
      double highClose = MathAbs(high[i] - close[i + 1]);
      double lowClose  = MathAbs(low[i] - close[i + 1]);
      double tr = MathMax(highLow, MathMax(highClose, lowClose));
      atr += tr;
   }

   atr /= period;
   return atr;
}


int SplitStringByDelimiters(string input_string, string &outputArray[])
{
   string cleaned = input_string;
   
      // Normalize: replace ',' with '|'
   StringReplace(cleaned, "+", "|");

   // Normalize: replace ',' with '|'
   StringReplace(cleaned, ",", "|");

   // Now split using '|'
   return StringSplit(cleaned, '|', outputArray);
}

void OpenAndClosePosition(string symbol, double lots)
{
    double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_ASK); // Get the current ask price
    double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_BID); // Get the current bid price

    if (ask == 0 || bid == 0)
    {
        Print("Error: Invalid market prices for ", symbol);
        return;
    }

    // Open a buy position
    if (trade.Buy(lots, symbol, ask, 0, 0, "Open and Close Test"))
    {
        ulong positionTicket = trade.ResultOrder(); // Get the ticket of the opened order
        PrintFormat("Position opened successfully: Symbol=%s, Ticket=%llu, Lots=%.2f", symbol, positionTicket, lots);

        // Close the position immediately
        Sleep(20000); // Optional: Wait 2 seconds for the position to be reflected
        if (PositionSelect(symbol)) // Select the position by symbol
        {
            double volume = PositionGetDouble(POSITION_VOLUME); // Get the position volume

            // Close the position using the ticket
            if (trade.PositionClose(symbol))
            {
                PrintFormat("Position closed successfully: Symbol=%s, Ticket=%llu, Volume=%.2f", symbol, positionTicket, volume);
            }
            else
            {
                PrintFormat("Failed to close position for %s. Error: %d", symbol, GetLastError());
            }
        }
        else
        {
            PrintFormat("Failed to select position for %s. Error: %d", symbol, GetLastError());
        }
    }
    else
    {
        PrintFormat("Failed to open position for %s. Error: %d", symbol, GetLastError());
    }
}


bool CheckTradesWithinLast25Days()
{
    datetime cutoffTime = TimeCurrent() - CheckTradesWithinLast * 86400; // 25 days in seconds

    // Select the trade history for the last 25 days
    if (!HistorySelect(cutoffTime, TimeCurrent()))
    {
        Print("Failed to select trade history. Error: ", GetLastError());
        return false;
    }

    // Get the total number of trades in the selected period
    int totalTrades = HistoryDealsTotal();
    //PrintFormat("Total trades in the last 25 days: %d", totalTrades);

    // Iterate through the trade history
    for (int i = 0; i < totalTrades; i++)
    {
        ulong dealTicket = HistoryDealGetTicket(i);
        if (dealTicket > 0)
        {
            // Get the deal's time and type
            datetime dealTime = HistoryDealGetInteger(dealTicket, DEAL_TIME);
            int dealType = HistoryDealGetInteger(dealTicket, DEAL_TYPE);

            // Check if the deal was opened within the last 25 days
            if ((dealType == DEAL_TYPE_BUY || dealType == DEAL_TYPE_SELL) && dealTime >= cutoffTime)
            {
                //PrintFormat("Trade Opened within the last 25 days. Time: %s, Ticket: %llu",
                //            TimeToString(dealTime, TIME_DATE | TIME_MINUTES), dealTicket);
                return true; // Found an opened trade within the last 25 days
            }
        }
    }

    //Print("No trades were opened within the last 25 days.");
    return false; // No opened trades within the period
}


void EnsureDatabaseExists(string dbFile)
{
    int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE | DATABASE_OPEN_CREATE);
    if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
    {
        Print("Failed to open database: ", dbFile, ". Error: ", GetLastError());
        return;
    }

    // Create an equity table if it does not exist
    string createTableQuery =
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS EquityData ("
        "Timestamp TEXT NOT NULL, "
        "Equity REAL NOT NULL)";
    
    if (!DatabaseExecute(db, createTableQuery))
    {
        Print("Failed to create table in database. Error: ", GetLastError());
    }
    
    DatabaseClose(db);
}


double CleanDBAndGetMaxEquity(string dbFile)
{
    // Open database
    int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE | DATABASE_OPEN_CREATE);
    if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
    {
        Print("Failed to open database: ", dbFile, ". Error: ", GetLastError());
        return -1;
    }

    // Ensure the table exists
    string createTableQuery =
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS EquityData ("
        "ID INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "
        "Timestamp INTEGER NOT NULL, "
        "Equity REAL NOT NULL)";
    
    if (!DatabaseExecute(db, createTableQuery))
    {
        Print("Failed to create table. Error: ", GetLastError());
        DatabaseClose(db);
        return -1;
    }

    // Calculate cutoff time (UNIX timestamp)
    datetime cutoffTime = TimeCurrent() - days_befor_delete_equity * 86400; // Convert days to seconds

    // Delete only old records (correct timestamp comparison)
    string deleteQuery = "DELETE FROM EquityData WHERE Timestamp < " + IntegerToString(cutoffTime);
    if (!DatabaseExecute(db, deleteQuery))
    {
        Print("Failed to delete old records. Error: ", GetLastError());
    }

    // Get max equity value
    string selectMaxQuery = "SELECT MAX(Equity) FROM EquityData";
    int stmt = DatabasePrepare(db, selectMaxQuery);
    
    double maxEquity = -DBL_MAX;
    if (stmt != INVALID_HANDLE)
    {
        if (DatabaseRead(stmt))
            DatabaseColumnDouble(stmt, 0, maxEquity);
        
        DatabaseFinalize(stmt);
    }
    
    DatabaseClose(db);
    return maxEquity;
}




void RecordEquityToDB(string dbFile)
{
    // Open or create database
    int db = DatabaseOpen(dbFile, DATABASE_OPEN_READWRITE | DATABASE_OPEN_CREATE);
    if (db == INVALID_HANDLE)
    {
        Print("Failed to open database: ", dbFile, ". Error: ", GetLastError());
        return;
    }

    // Ensure the table exists
    string createTableQuery =
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS EquityData ("
        "ID INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "
        "Timestamp INTEGER NOT NULL, "  // Store as UNIX timestamp
        "Equity REAL NOT NULL)";
    
    if (!DatabaseExecute(db, createTableQuery))
    {
        Print("Failed to create table. Error: ", GetLastError());
        DatabaseClose(db);
        return;
    }

    // Get current time and equity
    datetime now = TimeCurrent();
    double currentEquity = AccountInfoDouble(ACCOUNT_EQUITY);
    
    // Insert equity record
    string insertQuery = "INSERT INTO EquityData (Timestamp, Equity) VALUES (" +
                         IntegerToString(now) + ", " + DoubleToString(currentEquity, 2) + ")";
    
    if (!DatabaseExecute(db, insertQuery))
    {
        Print("Failed to insert equity data. Error: ", GetLastError());
    }

    DatabaseClose(db);
}


void EnsureFileExists(string filename)
{
    // Check if the file already exists
    if (FileIsExist(filename))
    {
        //Print("File already exists: ", filename);
        return;
    }

    // Try to create the file
    int handle = FileOpen(filename, FILE_WRITE | FILE_CSV | FILE_ANSI);
    if (handle != INVALID_HANDLE)
    {
        // Successfully created the file, now close it
        FileClose(handle);
        Print("File created: ", filename);
    }
    else
    {
        // If the file couldn't be created, log the error
        PrintFormat("Failed to create file. Error Code: %d, File: %s", GetLastError(), filename);
    }
}

bool IsErrorInList(int errorCode, const int &errorList[])
{
    for (int i = 0; i < ArraySize(errorList); i++)
    {
        if (errorList[i] == errorCode)
            return true;
    }
    return false;
}


void LogErrorToCSV()
{
    string mySpreadsheet = Filename_errors;

    int errorCode = GetLastError();
    if (errorCode == 0)
        return;
        
    if(!DontResetWhenManualCose && errorCode == 4753){
      return;
    }

    // Define and sort the list of error codes
    int errorList[] = {5031, 5126, 4307};
    ArraySort(errorList);

   if (IsErrorInList(errorCode, errorList)){
       return;  // Error not in the list
   }

    // Log to file (same as before)
    int handle = FileOpen(mySpreadsheet, FILE_READ | FILE_WRITE | FILE_CSV | FILE_ANSI);
    if (handle != INVALID_HANDLE)
    {
        FileSeek(handle, 0, SEEK_END);
        FileWrite(handle, TimeToString(TimeCurrent(), TIME_DATE | TIME_MINUTES | TIME_SECONDS), errorCode);
        FileClose(handle);

        PrintFormat("Logged error: %d at %s", errorCode, TimeToString(TimeCurrent(), TIME_DATE | TIME_MINUTES | TIME_SECONDS));
    }
    else
    {
        PrintFormat("Failed to open log file '%s'. Error: %d", mySpreadsheet, GetLastError());
    }
}



double PendingsVolume(string symbol)
{
    double volume_on_symbol = 0;
    ulong ticket;

    // Get the total number of currently placed orders
    int all_orders = OrdersTotal();

    // Iterate through all orders
    for (int i = 0; i < all_orders; i++)
    {
        // Get the ticket of an order by its position in the list
        if ((ticket = OrderGetTicket(i)))
        {
            // If our symbol is specified in the order, add the volume of this order
            if (symbol == OrderGetString(ORDER_SYMBOL))
                volume_on_symbol += OrderGetDouble(ORDER_VOLUME_INITIAL);
        }
    }

    // Return the total volume of currently placed pending orders for the specified symbol
    return (volume_on_symbol);
}

bool CanPlaceOrder(string symbol, double new_order_volume)
{
    // Get the current pending volume for the symbol
    double current_pending_volume = PendingsVolume(symbol);

    // Check against SYMBOL_VOLUME_LIMIT
    double symbol_volume_limit = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_VOLUME_LIMIT);
    if (symbol_volume_limit < 0)
    {
        Print("Failed to retrieve SYMBOL_VOLUME_LIMIT. Error: ", GetLastError());
        return false;
    }

    if (current_pending_volume + new_order_volume < symbol_volume_limit || symbol_volume_limit==0)
    {
       int all_orders = OrdersTotal() + PositionsTotal();
       if (all_orders < max_orders)
       {
           return true;
       }
       else{
         PrintFormat("Cannot place order. Total orders exceed limit: %d", max_orders);
       }
    }
    else{
      PrintFormat("Cannot place order. Exceeds SYMBOL_VOLUME_LIMIT: %.2f", symbol_volume_limit);
    }


    return false;
}

string ReadOrCreateSymbolsFile(const string fullPathFilename, const string inputstring)
{
   string result = "";
   string defaultSymbols = "";

   // Try to open the file for reading
   int fileHandle = FileOpen(fullPathFilename, FILE_READ | FILE_TXT | FILE_COMMON | FILE_ANSI);

   // If file doesn't exist, create it
   if(fileHandle == INVALID_HANDLE)
   {
      Print("File not found. Creating: ", fullPathFilename);

      fileHandle = FileOpen(fullPathFilename, FILE_WRITE | FILE_TXT | FILE_COMMON | FILE_ANSI);
      if(fileHandle == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         Print("Failed to create file: ", fullPathFilename, " Error: ", GetLastError());
         return _Symbol;
      }

      FileWrite(fileHandle, defaultSymbols);
      FileClose(fileHandle);

      // Try to reopen for reading
      fileHandle = FileOpen(fullPathFilename, FILE_READ | FILE_TXT | FILE_COMMON | FILE_ANSI);
      if(fileHandle == INVALID_HANDLE)
      {
         Print("Failed to reopen file: ", fullPathFilename, " Error: ", GetLastError());
         return _Symbol;
      }
   }

   // Read contents
   string fileContent = FileReadString(fileHandle);
   FileClose(fileHandle);

   // Normalize delimiters: replace '+' and ',' with '|'
   StringReplace(fileContent, "+", "|");
   StringReplace(fileContent, ",", "|");

   string cleanedInput = inputstring;
   StringReplace(cleanedInput, "+", "|");
   StringReplace(cleanedInput, ",", "|");

   if(StringLen(fileContent) == 0 && StringLen(cleanedInput) == 0)
   {
      Print("Input string is empty and the symbols file is empty.. Using current symbol: ", _Symbol);
      return _Symbol;
   }

   // Combine with new input
   if(StringLen(fileContent) != 0 && StringLen(cleanedInput) != 0){
      result = fileContent + "|" + cleanedInput;
   }
   else{
      if(StringLen(fileContent) == 0){
         result = cleanedInput;
      }
      else{
         if(StringLen(cleanedInput) == 0){
            result = fileContent;
         }
      }
   }

   StringReplace(result, " ", ""); // Remove spaces
   Print("File: ", fullPathFilename, " Symbols Loaded: ", result );

   // Split and remove duplicates
   string tempSymbols[];
   int count = StringSplit(result, '|', tempSymbols);
   if(count == 0)
   {
      Print("No symbols found in combined string.");
      return _Symbol;
   }

   string uniqueSymbols[];
   for(int i = 0; i < count; i++)
   {
      string s = tempSymbols[i];
      if(StringLen(s) == 0) continue;

      bool duplicate = false;
      for(int j = 0; j < ArraySize(uniqueSymbols); j++)
      {
         if(uniqueSymbols[j] == s)
         {
            duplicate = true;
            break;
         }
      }

      if(!duplicate)
      {
         int sz = ArraySize(uniqueSymbols);
         ArrayResize(uniqueSymbols, sz + 1);
         uniqueSymbols[sz] = s;
      }
   }

   // Rebuild result string
   result = uniqueSymbols[0];
   for(int i = 1; i < ArraySize(uniqueSymbols); i++)
      result += "|" + uniqueSymbols[i];

   return result;
}

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Custom SuperTrend calculation                                    |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
double GetCustomSuperTrend(const double &high[], const double &low[], const double &close[],
                           int period, double multiplier, double &outBand, bool &isUptrend)
{
   double atr = GetCustomATR(high, low, close, period);
   if (atr == EMPTY_VALUE) return EMPTY_VALUE;

   double hl2 = (high[0] + low[0]) / 2.0;
   double upperBand = hl2 + multiplier * atr;
   double lowerBand = hl2 - multiplier * atr;

   bool wasUptrend = close[1] > (high[1] + low[1]) / 2.0;

   if (wasUptrend)
   {
      if (close[0] < upperBand)
      {
         outBand = upperBand;
         isUptrend = false;
      }
      else
      {
         outBand = lowerBand;
         isUptrend = true;
      }
   }
   else
   {
      if (close[0] > lowerBand)
      {
         outBand = lowerBand;
         isUptrend = true;
      }
      else
      {
         outBand = upperBand;
         isUptrend = false;
      }
   }

   return outBand;
}

double ArrayAverageExcludingZeros(const double &array[])
{
    double sum = 0.0;
    int count = 0;

    for (int i = 0; i < ArraySize(array); i++)
    {
        if (array[i] != 0.0)
        {
            sum += array[i];
            count++;
        }
    }

    return (count > 0) ? (sum / count) : 0.0;
}


double iMAOnArray(double& array[], int period, int ma_shift, ENUM_MA_METHOD ma_method, int shift) {
   double buf[], arr[];
   int total = ArraySize(array);
   if(total <= period) return 0;
   if(shift > total - period - ma_shift) return 0;

   switch(ma_method) {
      case MODE_SMA: {
         total = ArrayCopy(arr, array, 0, shift + ma_shift, period);
         if (ArrayResize(buf, total) < 0) return 0;
         double sum = 0;
         int i, pos = total-1;
         for (i = 1; i < period; i++, pos--) sum += arr[pos];
         while (pos >= 0) {
            sum += arr[pos];
            buf[pos] = sum / period;
            sum -= arr[pos + period - 1];
            pos--;
         }
         return buf[0];
      }
      case MODE_EMA: {
         if (ArrayResize(buf, total) < 0) return 0;
         double pr = 2.0 / (period + 1);
         int pos = total - 2;
         while (pos >= 0) {
            if (pos == total - 2) buf[pos+1] = array[pos+1];
            buf[pos] = array[pos] * pr + buf[pos+1] * (1-pr);
            pos--;
         }
         return buf[shift+ma_shift];
      }
      case MODE_SMMA: {
         if (ArrayResize(buf, total) < 0) return(0);
         double sum = 0;
         int i, k, pos;
         pos = total - period;
         while (pos >= 0) {
            if (pos == total - period) {
               for (i = 0, k = pos; i < period; i++, k++) {
                  sum += array[k];
                  buf[k] = 0;
               }
            } else sum = buf[pos+1] * (period-1) + array[pos];
            buf[pos] = sum / period;
            pos--;
         }
         return buf[shift+ma_shift];
      }
      case MODE_LWMA: {
         if (ArrayResize(buf, total) < 0) return 0;
         double sum = 0.0, lsum = 0.0, price;
         int i, weight = 0, pos = total-1;
         for(i = 1; i <= period; i++, pos--) {
            price = array[pos];
            sum += price * i;
            lsum += price;
            weight += i;
         }
         pos++;
         i = pos + period;
         while (pos >= 0) {
            buf[pos] = sum / weight;
            if (pos == 0) break;
            pos--;
            i--;
            price = array[pos];
            sum = sum - lsum + price * period;
            lsum -= array[i];
            lsum += price;
         }
         return buf[shift+ma_shift];
      }
   }
   return 0;
}





int CalculateSlope(const double &hma_buffer[], const double &hma_buffer2[], const double multi, const int mainLength, int &result[]) {
    // Check input sizes
    int min_size = MathMin(ArraySize(hma_buffer), ArraySize(hma_buffer2)) - 1;
    if (min_size <= 0) {
        Print("Not enough data to calculate slopes.");
        return 0;
    }

    // Resize temporary arrays
    double sma_slope[], sma_slope2[];
    ArrayResize(sma_slope, min_size);
    ArrayResize(sma_slope2, min_size);

    // Calculate slopes
    for (int i = 0; i < min_size; i++) {
        sma_slope[i] = hma_buffer[i] - hma_buffer[i + 1];
        sma_slope2[i] = hma_buffer2[i] - hma_buffer2[i + 1];
    }

    // Calculate standard deviation values
    double stdev_values[];
    for (int i = mainLength - 1; i < ArraySize(sma_slope2); i++) {
        double stdev = PineStdev(sma_slope2, mainLength, i);
        ArrayResize(stdev_values, ArraySize(stdev_values) + 1);
        stdev_values[ArraySize(stdev_values) - 1] = stdev;
    }

    if (ArraySize(stdev_values) == 0) {
        Print("Standard deviation values not calculated.");
        return 0;
    }

    // Calculate normalized slopes
    double slope[];
    ArrayResize(slope, ArraySize(stdev_values));
    for (int i = 0; i < ArraySize(slope); i++) {
        slope[i] = sma_slope[i] / stdev_values[i];
    }

    // Separate positive and negative slopes
    double positive_slope[], negative_slope[];
    for (int i = 0; i < ArraySize(slope); i++) {
        if (slope[i] > 0) {
            ArrayResize(positive_slope, ArraySize(positive_slope) + 1);
            positive_slope[ArraySize(positive_slope) - 1] = slope[i];
        } else if (slope[i] < 0) {
            ArrayResize(negative_slope, ArraySize(negative_slope) + 1);
            negative_slope[ArraySize(negative_slope) - 1] = slope[i];
        }
    }

    // Check and calculate result array
    int slope_size = ArraySize(slope);
    if (slope_size > 0 && ArraySize(positive_slope) > 0 && ArraySize(negative_slope) > 0) {
        ArrayResize(result, slope_size);
        CheckSlope(slope, positive_slope, negative_slope, multi, result);
    } else {
        Print("Cannot calculate result due to empty slope arrays.");
        return 0;
    }

    // Successfully filled the result array
    return 1;
}





// Function to calculate the average of an array
double CalculateAverage(const double &array[]) {
    double sum = 0.0;
    int size = ArraySize(array);

    if (size == 0) {
        //if(ignorERROR1) {Print("Array is empty, returning 0 as average.");}
        return 0.0;  // Return 0 if the array is empty
    }

    for (int i = 0; i < size; i++) {
        sum += array[i];
    }

    return sum / size;  // Return the average
}


void CheckSlope(const double &slope[], const double &positive_slope[], const double &negative_slope[], const double multi, int &result[]) {
    int slopeSize = ArraySize(slope);

    if (slopeSize == 0) {
        Print("Slope array is empty. Exiting function.");
        return;  // Exit function if slope array is empty
    }

    // Resize the result array to match the size of the slope array
    ArrayResize(result, slopeSize);

    // Loop through the slope array
    for (int i = 0; i < slopeSize; i++) {
        // Get the average of the first 'i + 1' elements
        double positive_avg = CalculateAverage1(positive_slope, i + 1);
        double negative_avg = CalculateAverage1(negative_slope, i + 1);

        // Compare slope[i] with the calculated averages
        if (slope[i] > positive_avg * multi) {
            result[i] = 1;
        } else if (slope[i] < negative_avg * multi) {
            result[i] = -1;
        } else {
            result[i] = 0;
        }
    }
}

// Helper function to calculate average of first `count` elements of an array
double CalculateAverage1(const double &array[], int count) {
   
    if (count > ArraySize(array)) count = ArraySize(array); // Ensure count doesn't exceed array size
    if (count <= 0) return 0.0;

    double sum = 0.0;
    for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
        sum += array[i];
    }
    return sum / count;
}



// Helper function: Check if a value is near zero
bool IsZero(double val, double eps) {
    return (MathAbs(val) <= eps);
}

// Helper function: Custom SUM logic
double SUM(double fst, double snd) {
    const double EPS = 1e-10;
    double res = fst + snd;

    if (IsZero(res, EPS)) {
        res = 0.0;
    } else {
        if (!IsZero(res, 1e-4)) {
            res = res;
        } else {
            res = 15.0;
        }
    }

    return res;
}

// Main function: Calculate standard deviation similar to Pine Script
double PineStdev(const double &src[], int length, int index) {
    // Check valid length
    if (length <= 0 || index < length - 1) {
        Print("Invalid length or index out of range");
        return 0.0;
    }

    // Calculate the average (sma)
    double avg = 0.0;
    for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
        avg += src[index - i];
    }
    avg /= length;

    // Calculate the sum of squared deviations
    double sumOfSquareDeviations = 0.0;
    for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
        double sum = SUM(src[index - i], -avg);
        sumOfSquareDeviations += sum * sum;
    }

    // Calculate and return the standard deviation
    double stdev = MathSqrt(sumOfSquareDeviations / length);
    return stdev;
}



void CloseAllOrders2(string tableName, ulong originalID) {
    ulong closedTickets[]; // Dynamic array to store successfully closed tickets
    bool allClosed = true; // Flag to track if all tickets are successfully closed
             // Array to store the resulting PositionIDs
      int positionIDs[];
   
      // Call the function to find PositionIDs for the given OriginalID
      FindPositionIDsByOriginalID(dbFile, originalID, positionIDs);
   
      // Output the PositionIDs
      if(ArraySize(positionIDs) > 0)
      {
         //Print("PositionIDs found for OriginalID=", originalID, ":");
         for(int i = 0; i < ArraySize(positionIDs); i++)
         {
            //Print("PositionID[", i, "] = ", positionIDs[i]);
         }
      }
      else
      {
         Print("error? No PositionIDs found for OriginalID=", originalID);
      }
         for (int j = 0; j < ArraySize(positionIDs); j++)
         {
            ulong ticket = positionIDs[j];
            // Check if the position exists for the given ticket
            if (PositionSelectByTicket(ticket)){
               // Attempt to close the position
               if (trade.PositionClose(ticket)){
                  Print("Position closed successfully for ticket: ", ticket);
      
                  // Add the successfully closed ticket to the `closedTickets` array
                  int newSize = ArraySize(closedTickets) + 1;
                  ArrayResize(closedTickets, newSize);
                  closedTickets[newSize - 1] = ticket; // Add ticket to the last index
               }
               else
               {
                  Print("Failed to close ticket: ", ticket);
                  allClosed = false; // Set flag to false if a ticket couldn't be closed
               }
            }
            else
            {
               bool isClosed = IsOrderClosed(ticket);
               if(isClosed){
                  Print("ticket was already closed: ", ticket);
                  int newSize = ArraySize(closedTickets) + 1;
                  ArrayResize(closedTickets, newSize);
                  closedTickets[newSize - 1] = ticket; // Add ticket to the last index
               }
               else
               {
                  Print("The order with ticket ", ticket, " is NOT closed or doesn't exist.");
               }
            }
         }
       // Only call resetOrder if all tickets were successfully closed
       if (allClosed) {
         DeleteRowsByPositionIDArray(dbFile, positionIDs);
       } else {
           Print("an error happended when closing an order.");
       }
}


bool IsOrderClosed(ulong ticket)
{
   // First, check if the order is currently open
   if (OrderSelect(ticket))
   {
      // If order is found in open positions, it is not closed
      Print("Order is still open. Ticket: ", ticket);
      return false;
   }

   // If not in open positions, check the history
   if (HistorySelect(0, TimeCurrent())) // Load the full history
   {
      for (int i = 0; i < HistoryOrdersTotal(); i++)
      {
         ulong historyTicket = HistoryOrderGetTicket(i);
         if (historyTicket == ticket)
         {
            // Retrieve ORDER_TIME_DONE to determine if it's closed
            datetime closeTime = (datetime)HistoryOrderGetInteger(ticket, ORDER_TIME_DONE);
            return closeTime != 0; // If closeTime is 0, the order is not closed
         }
      }
   }

   // If not found in open positions or history, return false
   Print("Order ticket ", ticket, " not found.");
   return false;
}

void update_open_symbol3(int SymbolLoop)
{
    string symbol = SymbolArray3[SymbolLoop];
    double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_BID);
    double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_ASK);
    double mid = (ask + bid) / 2;

    bool session_active = false;
    datetime currentTime = TimeCurrent();

    // Get the current day of the week
    MqlDateTime timeStruct;
    TimeToStruct(currentTime, timeStruct);
    ENUM_DAY_OF_WEEK currentDay = (ENUM_DAY_OF_WEEK)timeStruct.day_of_week;

    // Loop through all possible sessions for the current day
    uint sessionIndex = 0;
    datetime openTime, closeTime;
   while (SymbolInfoSessionTrade(symbol, currentDay, sessionIndex, openTime, closeTime))
   {
       // Convert session times to absolute datetime for comparison
       datetime sessionOpen = currentTime - currentTime % 86400 + openTime;
       datetime sessionClose = currentTime - currentTime % 86400 + closeTime;
   
       // Adjust for sessions that cross midnight
       if (sessionClose < sessionOpen)
           sessionClose += 86400;
   
       // Check if the current time falls within the session
       if (currentTime >= sessionOpen && currentTime <= sessionClose)
       {
           session_active = true;
           break; // Exit loop once a valid session is found
       }
   
       sessionIndex++; // Move to the next session
   }

    // Check if there's no previous mid-price
    if (open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][0] == 0)
    {
        open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][0] = mid;   // Set initial mid-price
        open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][1] = 0;    // Reset indicator to 0
        open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][2] = 0;    // Timer starts at 0 seconds
    }
    else
    {
        if (open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][0] != mid && session_active)
        {
            // If the mid-price has changed
            open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][0] = mid;   // Update mid-price
            open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][1] = 1;     // Set indicator to 1
            open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][2] = countdownInterval;  // Set timer to countdownInterval
        }
        else
        {
            // If the mid-price hasn't changed, decrement the timer
            if (open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][2] > 0)
            {
                open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][2] -= RecordingInterval; // Decrease the timer
            }

            // If the timer reaches 0, reset the indicator
            if (open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][2] <= 0)
            {
                open_symbols3[SymbolLoop][1] = 0; // Reset indicator to 0
            }
        }
    }
}


void update_open_symbol4(int SymbolLoop)
{
    string symbol = SymbolArray4[SymbolLoop];
    double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_BID);
    double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_ASK);
    double mid = (ask + bid) / 2;

    bool session_active = false;
    datetime currentTime = TimeCurrent();

    // Get the current day of the week
    MqlDateTime timeStruct;
    TimeToStruct(currentTime, timeStruct);
    ENUM_DAY_OF_WEEK currentDay = (ENUM_DAY_OF_WEEK)timeStruct.day_of_week;
    // Loop through all possible sessions for the current day
    uint sessionIndex = 0;
    datetime openTime, closeTime;
   while (SymbolInfoSessionTrade(symbol, currentDay, sessionIndex, openTime, closeTime))
   {
       // Convert session times to absolute datetime for comparison
       datetime sessionOpen = currentTime - currentTime % 86400 + openTime;
       datetime sessionClose = currentTime - currentTime % 86400 + closeTime;
   
       // Adjust for sessions that cross midnight
       if (sessionClose < sessionOpen)
           sessionClose += 86400;
   
       // Check if the current time falls within the session
       if (currentTime >= sessionOpen && currentTime <= sessionClose)
       {
           session_active = true;
           break; // Exit loop once a valid session is found
       }
   
       sessionIndex++; // Move to the next session
   }

    // Check if there's no previous mid-price
    if (open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][0] == 0)
    {
        open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][0] = mid;   // Set initial mid-price
        open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][1] = 0;    // Reset indicator to 0
        open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][2] = 0;    // Timer starts at 0 seconds
    }
    else
    {
        if (open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][0] != mid && session_active)
        {
            // If the mid-price has changed
            open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][0] = mid;   // Update mid-price
            open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][1] = 1;     // Set indicator to 1
            open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][2] = countdownInterval;  // Set timer to countdownInterval
        }
        else
        {
            // If the mid-price hasn't changed, decrement the timer
            if (open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][2] > 0)
            {
                open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][2] -= RecordingInterval; // Decrease the timer
            }

            // If the timer reaches 0, reset the indicator
            if (open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][2] <= 0)
            {
                open_symbols4[SymbolLoop][1] = 0; // Reset indicator to 0
            }
        }
    }
}   


void update_open_symbol5(int SymbolLoop)
{
    string symbol = SymbolArray5[SymbolLoop];
    double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_BID);
    double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_ASK);
    double mid = (ask + bid) / 2;

    bool session_active = false;
    datetime currentTime = TimeCurrent();

    // Get the current day of the week
    MqlDateTime timeStruct;
    TimeToStruct(currentTime, timeStruct);
    ENUM_DAY_OF_WEEK currentDay = (ENUM_DAY_OF_WEEK)timeStruct.day_of_week;

    // Loop through all possible sessions for the current day
    uint sessionIndex = 0;
    datetime openTime, closeTime;
   while (SymbolInfoSessionTrade(symbol, currentDay, sessionIndex, openTime, closeTime))
   {
       // Convert session times to absolute datetime for comparison
       datetime sessionOpen = currentTime - currentTime % 86400 + openTime;
       datetime sessionClose = currentTime - currentTime % 86400 + closeTime;
   
       // Adjust for sessions that cross midnight
       if (sessionClose < sessionOpen)
           sessionClose += 86400;
   
       // Check if the current time falls within the session
       if (currentTime >= sessionOpen && currentTime <= sessionClose)
       {
           session_active = true;
           break; // Exit loop once a valid session is found
       }
   
       sessionIndex++; // Move to the next session
   }

    // Check if there's no previous mid-price
    if (open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][0] == 0)
    {
        open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][0] = mid;   // Set initial mid-price
        open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][1] = 0;    // Reset indicator to 0
        open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][2] = 0;    // Timer starts at 0 seconds
    }
    else
    {
        if (open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][0] != mid && session_active)
        {
            // If the mid-price has changed
            open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][0] = mid;   // Update mid-price
            open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][1] = 1;     // Set indicator to 1
            open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][2] = countdownInterval;  // Set timer to countdownInterval
        }
        else
        {
            // If the mid-price hasn't changed, decrement the timer
            if (open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][2] > 0)
            {
                open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][2] -= RecordingInterval; // Decrease the timer
            }

            // If the timer reaches 0, reset the indicator
            if (open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][2] <= 0)
            {
                open_symbols5[SymbolLoop][1] = 0; // Reset indicator to 0
            }
        }
    }
}

void update_open_symbol8(int SymbolLoop)
{
    string symbol = SymbolArray8[SymbolLoop];
    double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_BID);
    double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_ASK);
    double mid = (ask + bid) / 2;

    bool session_active = false;
    datetime currentTime = TimeCurrent();

    // Get the current day of the week
    MqlDateTime timeStruct;
    TimeToStruct(currentTime, timeStruct);
    ENUM_DAY_OF_WEEK currentDay = (ENUM_DAY_OF_WEEK)timeStruct.day_of_week;
    // Loop through all possible sessions for the current day
    uint sessionIndex = 0;
    datetime openTime, closeTime;
   while (SymbolInfoSessionTrade(symbol, currentDay, sessionIndex, openTime, closeTime))
   {
       // Convert session times to absolute datetime for comparison
       datetime sessionOpen = currentTime - currentTime % 86400 + openTime;
       datetime sessionClose = currentTime - currentTime % 86400 + closeTime;
   
       // Adjust for sessions that cross midnight
       if (sessionClose < sessionOpen)
           sessionClose += 86400;
   
       // Check if the current time falls within the session
       if (currentTime >= sessionOpen && currentTime <= sessionClose)
       {
           session_active = true;
           break; // Exit loop once a valid session is found
       }
   
       sessionIndex++; // Move to the next session
   }

    // Check if there's no previous mid-price
    if (open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][0] == 0)
    {
        open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][0] = mid;   // Set initial mid-price
        open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][1] = 0;    // Reset indicator to 0
        open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][2] = 0;    // Timer starts at 0 seconds
    }
    else
    {
        if (open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][0] != mid && session_active)
        {
            // If the mid-price has changed
            open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][0] = mid;   // Update mid-price
            open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][1] = 1;     // Set indicator to 1
            open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][2] = countdownInterval;  // Set timer to countdownInterval
        }
        else
        {
            // If the mid-price hasn't changed, decrement the timer
            if (open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][2] > 0)
            {
                open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][2] -= RecordingInterval; // Decrease the timer
            }

            // If the timer reaches 0, reset the indicator
            if (open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][2] <= 0)
            {
                open_symbols8[SymbolLoop][1] = 0; // Reset indicator to 0
            }
        }
    }
}   

void update_open_symbol11(int SymbolLoop)
{
    string symbol = SymbolArray11[SymbolLoop];
    double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_BID);
    double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_ASK);
    double mid = (ask + bid) / 2;

    bool session_active = false;
    datetime currentTime = TimeCurrent();

    // Get the current day of the week
    MqlDateTime timeStruct;
    TimeToStruct(currentTime, timeStruct);
    ENUM_DAY_OF_WEEK currentDay = (ENUM_DAY_OF_WEEK)timeStruct.day_of_week;
    // Loop through all possible sessions for the current day
    uint sessionIndex = 0;
    datetime openTime, closeTime;
   while (SymbolInfoSessionTrade(symbol, currentDay, sessionIndex, openTime, closeTime))
   {
       // Convert session times to absolute datetime for comparison
       datetime sessionOpen = currentTime - currentTime % 86400 + openTime;
       datetime sessionClose = currentTime - currentTime % 86400 + closeTime;
   
       // Adjust for sessions that cross midnight
       if (sessionClose < sessionOpen)
           sessionClose += 86400;
   
       // Check if the current time falls within the session
       if (currentTime >= sessionOpen && currentTime <= sessionClose)
       {
           session_active = true;
           break; // Exit loop once a valid session is found
       }
   
       sessionIndex++; // Move to the next session
   }

    // Check if there's no previous mid-price
    if (open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][0] == 0)
    {
        open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][0] = mid;   // Set initial mid-price
        open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][1] = 0;    // Reset indicator to 0
        open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][2] = 0;    // Timer starts at 0 seconds
    }
    else
    {
        if (open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][0] != mid && session_active)
        {
            // If the mid-price has changed
            open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][0] = mid;   // Update mid-price
            open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][1] = 1;     // Set indicator to 1
            open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][2] = countdownInterval;  // Set timer to countdownInterval
        }
        else
        {
            // If the mid-price hasn't changed, decrement the timer
            if (open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][2] > 0)
            {
                open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][2] -= RecordingInterval; // Decrease the timer
            }

            // If the timer reaches 0, reset the indicator
            if (open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][2] <= 0)
            {
                open_symbols11[SymbolLoop][1] = 0; // Reset indicator to 0
            }
        }
    }
}

void update_open_symbol13(int SymbolLoop)
{
    string symbol = SymbolArray13[SymbolLoop];
    double bid = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_BID);
    double ask = SymbolInfoDouble(symbol, SYMBOL_ASK);
    double mid = (ask + bid) / 2;

    bool session_active = false;
    datetime currentTime = TimeCurrent();

    // Get the current day of the week
    MqlDateTime timeStruct;
    TimeToStruct(currentTime, timeStruct);
    ENUM_DAY_OF_WEEK currentDay = (ENUM_DAY_OF_WEEK)timeStruct.day_of_week;
    // Loop through all possible sessions for the current day
    uint sessionIndex = 0;
    datetime openTime, closeTime;
   while (SymbolInfoSessionTrade(symbol, currentDay, sessionIndex, openTime, closeTime))
   {
       // Convert session times to absolute datetime for comparison
       datetime sessionOpen = currentTime - currentTime % 86400 + openTime;
       datetime sessionClose = currentTime - currentTime % 86400 + closeTime;
   
       // Adjust for sessions that cross midnight
       if (sessionClose < sessionOpen)
           sessionClose += 86400;
   
       // Check if the current time falls within the session
       if (currentTime >= sessionOpen && currentTime <= sessionClose)
       {
           session_active = true;
           break; // Exit loop once a valid session is found
       }
   
       sessionIndex++; // Move to the next session
   }

    // Check if there's no previous mid-price
    if (open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][0] == 0)
    {
        open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][0] = mid;   // Set initial mid-price
        open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][1] = 0;    // Reset indicator to 0
        open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][2] = 0;    // Timer starts at 0 seconds
    }
    else
    {
        if (open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][0] != mid && session_active)
        {
            // If the mid-price has changed
            open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][0] = mid;   // Update mid-price
            open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][1] = 1;     // Set indicator to 1
            open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][2] = countdownInterval;  // Set timer to countdownInterval
        }
        else
        {
            // If the mid-price hasn't changed, decrement the timer
            if (open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][2] > 0)
            {
                open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][2] -= RecordingInterval; // Decrease the timer
            }

            // If the timer reaches 0, reset the indicator
            if (open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][2] <= 0)
            {
                open_symbols13[SymbolLoop][1] = 0; // Reset indicator to 0
            }
        }
    }
}
